<?xml version='1.0' encoding='UTF-8'?>
<!DOCTYPE sailpoint PUBLIC "sailpoint.dtd" "sailpoint.dtd">
<sailpoint>
<Workflow explicitTransitions="true" libraries="Identity" name="Lifecycle Event - Manager Approval for all native changes" type="IdentityLifecycle">
  <Variable input="true" name="trigger">
    <Description>The IdentityTrigger</Description>
  </Variable>
  <Variable input="true" name="event" transient="true">
    <Description>
      The IdentityChangeEvent.  It can be used to build
      the provisioning plan, but does not need to be
      persisted with the case, so marked as transient.
    </Description>
  </Variable>
  <Variable input="true" name="identityName">
    <Description>The name of the identity.</Description>
  </Variable>
  
  <Variable initializer="script:(identityDisplayName != void) ? identityDisplayName : resolveDisplayName(identityName)" input="true" name="identityDisplayName">
    <Description>
      The displayName of the identity being updated.
      Query for this using a projection query and fall back to the name.
    </Description>
  </Variable>
  <Variable name="plan">
    <Description>The provisioning plan, which is built by a service method. </Description>
  </Variable>
  <Variable editable="true" initializer="false" name="optimisticProvisioning">
    <Description>
      Set to true to enable optimistic provisioning.  This will cause
      changes to the entitlements compiled from role assignments to be 
      applied immediately to the identity cube rather than waiting
      for the next refresh/reaggregation after the provisioning system
      completes the request.
    </Description>
  </Variable>
 
 <Variable editable="true" initializer="true" name="foregroundProvisioning">
    <Description>
      Normally provisioning is done in a step that uses the "background"
      option to force the workflow to be suspend and be resumed in a
      background task thread.  This prevents the browser session from
      hanging since provision can sometimes take a long time.  For demos
      and testing it can be better to do this in the foreground so that
      provisioning will have been performed when control is returned to the
      user.  This prevents having to run the Perform Maintenance task to 
      see the results of the request.
    </Description>
  </Variable>
  
  <Variable initializer="spadmin" input="true" name="fallbackApprover">
    <Description>
      A String that specifies the name of the Identity that will 
      be assigned any approvals where the owner of the approver 
      can't be resolved. Example if the scheme is "owner" and the 
      application doesn't specify and owner.
    </Description>
  </Variable>
  
  <Variable initializer="LCM" input="true" name="source">
    <Description>
      String version of sailpoint.object.Source to indicate
      where the request originated.  Defaults to LCM.
    </Description>
  </Variable>
  
  <Variable initializer="false" input="true" name="trace">
    <Description>
      Used for debugging this workflow and when set to true trace
      will be sent to stdout.
    </Description>
  </Variable>
  
  <Variable name="project">
    <Description>
      ProvisioningProject which is just a compiled version of the ProvisioningPlan.
    </Description>
  </Variable>
  
  <Variable name="identityRequestId" output="true">
    <Description>
       The sequence id of the Identity request object which is stored in 
       the name field of the identity request.
    </Description>
  </Variable>
  
  <Variable name="approvalSet">
    <Description>
       The variable used to hold the approval set generated from the
       native changes on the event.
    </Description>
  </Variable>
  
  <Variable initializer="true" name="provisionRejectedItems">
    <Description>
        Flag to indicate if actual provisioning to reverse te native
        change should take place OR if it should just print a plan to 
        stdout. Set this variable to true, if you want it to provision
        the rejected items, otherwise it'll just be printed to stdout. 
     </Description>
  </Variable>
  <Variable name="launcher">
    <Description>The name of the identity that launched the workflow. In cases where workflows are launched by the system an alternate launcher name may be passed as as a variable.</Description>
  </Variable>
  <Variable initializer="Modify" name="operations">
    <Description>CSV list of operations that are part of the native change request, default to Modify but this will be recalculated in the "Build OP String" step.</Description>
  </Variable>
  <Variable initializer="Normal" input="true" name="workItemPriority">
    <Description>
       The String version of a WorkItem.Priority. This variable is 
       used to set the priority on all of the workitems generated 
       as part of this workflow and also set on the IdentityRequest
       object.
    </Description>
  </Variable>
  <Description>
  An example workflow that requires manager approval
  for all natively detected changes found by IdentityIQ.
  
  Any items rejected by the manager will be reversed and 
  provisioned.    
  </Description>
  <RuleLibraries>
    <Reference class="sailpoint.object.Rule" name="LCM Workflow Library"/>
  </RuleLibraries>
  <Step icon="Start" name="start" posX="23" posY="129">
    <Script>
      <Source>
        import sailpoint.tools.Util;
        if ( Util.otob(trace) ) { 
            System.out.println("Event was fired for identity ["+identityName+"]");
            System.out.println("                    trigger ["+trigger.toXml()+"]");
            System.out.println("                    event ["+event.toXml()+"]");
        }
      </Source>
    </Script>
    <Transition to="Build Op String"/>
    <Transition to="end" when="script:(Util.size(event.getNativeChanges())==0)"/>
  </Step>
  <Step name="Build Op String" posX="81" posY="20" resultVariable="operations">
    <Script>
      <Source>
        import sailpoint.object.NativeChangeDetection;
        import sailpoint.object.ProvisioningPlan.AccountRequest;
        import sailpoint.tools.Util;
        import sailpoint.object.AttributeChange;
import sailpoint.object.AttributeChange.ObjectOperation;

        List ops = new ArrayList();

if (event != null) {
    List ncs = event.getNativeChanges();
    if (ncs != null) {
        
        // 1. Loop mein generic 'Object' ka use kiya standard casting ke liye
        for (Object obj : ncs) {
            AttributeChange nc = (AttributeChange) obj;
            
            // 2. AccountRequest.Operation ki jagah AttributeChange.ObjectOperation use kiya
            ObjectOperation op = nc.getOperation();
            String opString = ""; // 3. Variable ko loop ke andar declare kiya
            
            if (op == null) {
                opString = "Modify";
            } else {
                opString = op.toString(); // Yeh "Set", "Add", ya "Remove" return karega
            }

            if (!ops.contains(opString)) {
                ops.add(opString);
            }
        }
    }
}

// Ops list ko Comma-Separated String (CSV) mein convert karke return karega (e.g., "Set,Add")
return Util.listToCsv(ops);
      </Source>
    </Script>
    <Transition to="Build Native Change Approval"/>
  </Step>
  <Step action="call:buildApprovalSetFromNativeChanges" name="Build Native Change Approval" posX="232" posY="20" resultVariable="approvalSet">
    <Arg name="event" value="ref:event"/>
    <Return name="approvalSet" to="approvalSet"/>
    <Transition to="Approve Native Change"/>
  </Step>
  <Step name="Approve Native Change" posX="408" posY="20">
    <Approval mode="parallel" owner="script:getManagerName(identityName, launcher, fallbackApprover);" 
	renderer="nativeChangeApprovalRenderer.xhtml" send="identityDisplayName,identityName">
      <AfterScript>
        <Source>
          import sailpoint.workflow.IdentityRequestLibrary;
                    
          if ( item == null ) 
              return;

          assimilateWorkItemApprovalSet(wfcontext, item, approvalSet);          
          auditDecisions(item);
        </Source>
      </AfterScript>
      <Arg name="workItemRequester" value="$(launcher)"/>
      <Arg name="launcher" value="ref:launcher"/>
      <Arg name="approvalSet" value="ref:approvalSet"/>
      <Arg name="operations" value="$(operations)"/>
      <Arg name="workItemDescription" value="Native Account Changes for User: $(identityDisplayName) - Manager Approval"/>
      <Arg name="workItemNotificationTemplate" value="ref:ownerEmailTemplate"/>
      <Arg name="workItemPriority" value="ref:workItemPriority"/>
    </Approval>
    <Transition to="Process Approval Decisions"/>
  </Step>
  <Step action="call:processNativeChangesApprovalDecisions" name="Process Approval Decisions" posX="575" posY="20" resultVariable="plan">
    <Transition to="Provision Native Change Reversal"/>
  </Step>
  <Step condition="script:( Util.otob(provisionRejectedItems) &amp;&amp; plan != null )" icon="Task" name="Provision Native Change Reversal" posX="767" posY="20">
    <Arg name="flow" value="EntitlementsRequest"/>
    <Arg name="identityName" value="ref:identityName"/>
    <Arg name="identityDisplayName" value="ref:identityDisplayName"/>
    <Arg name="optimisticProvisioning" value="ref:optimisticProvisioning"/>
    <Arg name="plan" value="ref:plan"/>
    <Arg name="policyScheme" value="none"/>
    <Arg name="priority" value="ref:workItemPriority"/>
    <Arg name="approvalScheme" value="none"/>
    <Arg name="source" value="ref:source"/>
    <Arg name="requireViolationReviewComments" value="false"/>
    <Arg name="allowRequestsWithViolations" value="true"/>
    <Arg name="enableRetryRequest" value="false"/>
    <Arg name="launcher" value="ref:launcher"/>
    <Arg name="doRefresh" value="true"/>
    <Arg name="trace" value="ref:trace"/>
    <Return name="project" to="project"/>
    <Return name="identityRequestId" to="identityRequestId"/>
    <Return merge="true" name="workItemComments" to="workItemComments"/>
    <WorkflowRef>
      <Reference class="sailpoint.object.Workflow" name="LCM Provisioning"/>
    </WorkflowRef>
    <Transition to="end"/>
  </Step>
  <Step catches="complete" icon="Catches" name="Complete" posX="658" posY="185">
    <Arg name="priority" value="ref:workItemPriority"/>
    <Arg name="project" value="ref:project"/>
    <Arg name="trace" value="ref:trace"/>
    <Arg name="approvalSet" value="ref:approvalSet"/>
    <Arg name="identityRequestId" value="ref:identityRequestId"/>
    <Description>
      Call the standard subprocess that can audit/finalize the request if they are in play. 
    </Description>
    <WorkflowRef>
      <Reference class="sailpoint.object.Workflow" name="Identity Request Finalize"/>
    </WorkflowRef>
    <Transition to="end"/>
  </Step>
  <Step icon="Stop" name="end" posX="767" posY="125"/>
</Workflow>
</sailpoint>
/////////////*
<Script> step ke shuru hone par ya step ke dauran chalta hai (Action lene ke liye).

<AfterScript> step ke poora khatam hone ke thik baad chalta hai (Cleaning ya confirmation ke liye).

<ValidationScript>

()<Workflow explicitTransitions="true"
          libraries="Identity"
          name="Lifecycle Event - Manager Approval for all native changes"
          type="IdentityLifecycle">:-
()Workflow:-
Ye main workflow object hai jo poora process define karta hai.
Jaise:-
approval
provisioning
joiner/mover/leaver
lifecycle events
identity update
access request
sab workflow ke andar hota hai.

(). explicitTransitions="true":-
Ye Workflow attribute/property hai.
Ye control karta hai workflow ka flow automatic hoga ya manually.
<Workflow explicitTransitions="true">
Matlab:-
next step manually define karna padega
<Transition to="..."/> use karna padega

(). libraries="Identity":-
Ye workflow library use karta hai.
Identity library me prebuilt methods/functions provide  karta hai workflow ke andar.
Example:-
identity lookup
manager fetch
attribute handling
provisioning utilities
Workflow me directly use kar sakte ho.
Example:-
<Workflow libraries="Identity">
Matlab Identity related helper methods available hain.

(). type="IdentityLifecycle":-
Ye workflow ka category/type define karta hai.
IdentityLifecycle ka matlab:-
Ye Identity Lifecycle Event ke liye use hota hai.
Jaise:-
Joiner
Mover
Leaver
Identity update
Access change
Lifecycle manager workflows isi type ke hote hain.

()SailPoint me Common Libraries:-
Library	              Use
Identity:-------Identity operations
Role:-----------Role operations
PolicyViolation----Policy handling
LCM----------------Lifecycle management
*///////////
////////////*
()<Variable input="true" name="trigger">
--Variable:-Ye workflow variable declare karta hai.

--input="true":-
Matlab Ye variable workflow start hote time bahar se value receive karega.
Input variable hai.

--name="trigger":-
Variable ka naam trigger hai.
Is variable me usually:-
IdentityTrigger object
lifecycle trigger info
store hota hai.
Example:-
joiner trigger
mover trigger
native change trigger

()<Variable input="true"
          name="event"
          transient="true">
Matlab:-
Workflow ek temporary input variable lega jiska naam event hai aur DB me persist nahi karega.

--Ye usually:-
IdentityChangeEvent object hota hai.

Isme:-
native changes
operations
changed attributes
sab hota hai.

()transient="true"->db me save(persist) nahi hoga.

()<Variable input="true" name="identityName">:-
name="identityName"
Variable ka naam identityName hai.
Ye store karta hai:-
identity ka naam
user name
Example:-
kishan.singh
john.doe
spadmin
-----------------------------------------------------
()1. IdentityTrigger kya hai?
IdentityTrigger ek object hai jo batata hai:-
Workflow kis reason/event ki wajah se trigger hua.

Simple Meaning:-
Jaise alarm trigger hota hai.
Waise hi IIQ me:-
joiner
mover
leaver
attribute change
manager change
native change
hone pe workflow trigger hota hai.

()Us trigger ki details:-
IdentityTrigger object me hoti hain.

Example:-
Suppose:-
Department changed
IT → Finance
Toh lifecycle event trigger hoga.

()IdentityTrigger object me info ho sakti hai:-
Field	            Value
Trigger Name------Department Change
Type--------------Lifecycle Event
Condition---------department changed
Enabled-------------true

Code me:-
trigger.getName()
trigger.getType()
----------------------------------------------------
()2. Lifecycle Trigger Info kya hota hai?
Ye koi exact class name nahi.
Ye meaning hai:-
Lifecycle event ki information.
Example Lifecycle Events:-
Event	              Example
Joiner--------------New employee
Mover---------------Department changed
Leaver--------------Employee resigned
Manager Change------New manager assigned
Native Change-------Target system me direct change

()Trigger Info me kya ho sakta hai?
kis event pe workflow chala,
kis identity pe chala,
kaunsa rule match hua,
kya condition thi.
------------------------------------------------------
()3. IdentityChangeEvent kya hai?
Ye bahut important object hai.
IdentityChangeEvent object store karta hai:-
Identity me kya changes detect hue.

Example:-
Suppose AD account me:-
title change
department change
entitlement add
hua.

Toh uski details:-
IdentityChangeEvent me aayegi.

Isme kya hota hai?
Data	                Example
Changed attributes-----department
Old value-----------------IT
New value---------------Finance
Native changes--------entitlement added
Operations-----------Modify/Create/Delete
*///////////
////////////*
()<Variable 
initializer="script:(identityDisplayName != void) ? identityDisplayName : resolveDisplayName(identityName)" 
input="true" name="identityDisplayName">:-

--1. Variable:-Workflow variable declare kar raha hai.

--2. initializer="...":-
Initializer ka matlab:-Default value set karna.
Agar variable me value nahi aayi toh ye logic chalega.

--3. script:
Matlab:-Initializer simple text nahi hai,Ye script execute karega.

4.(identityDisplayName != void):-
Ye condition check kar raha hai.
Meaning:-Kya identityDisplayName already available hai ya nahi.

--void:-Workflow scripting me,null/empty/not present jaisa use hota hai.

6.identityDisplayName:-Agar value already hai toh wahi use karo.

--8.resolveDisplayName(identityName):-
Agar identityDisplayName nahi mila:-
Toh:-
identityName use karke display name find karo.

()resolveDisplayName():-
Ye helper method/function hai.
Ye usually:-
identity lookup karta hai,display name return karta hai.

()9. input="true":-Workflow bahar se bhi value receive kar sakta hai.

()10. name="identityDisplayName":-Variable ka naam.
*//////////
//////////*
()<Variable name="plan">
Matlab:-
plan naam ka variable banao.
Abhi isme value nahi hai.

()"plan ko value kaha se milegi?"
Workflow ke dusre step se.
Ye step dekho

-->plan ko value ish step se milegi.
<Step action="call:processNativeChangesApprovalDecisions"
      name="Process Approval Decisions"
      resultVariable="plan">
--resultVariable="plan":-
Matlab:-
Is step ka return result plan variable me store karo.

-->1. Step:-Ye workflow ka ek execution block/stage hai.

-->2.action:-Workflow ko batata hai ki Ish step me kya execute karna hai.

-->3.call:-
Matlab:-Kisi method/function/library action ko call karo.

-->4.processNativeChangesApprovalDecisions:-
Ye method/action ka naam hai.
Usually:-
workflow library method
rule library method
predefined SailPoint method hi likh sakte ho action me.
--Ye Method Mainly Kya Karta Hai?
1. Approval Decisions Read karta hai
ApprovalSet check karta hai.
Example:-
Item	             Decision
Add Finance Group----Rejected
Remove HR Group------Approved

2. Rejected Items Identify karta hai
Manager ne kya reject kiya:-
jaise:-
Rejected entitlement
Rejected attribute update
Rejected account change

3. Reverse Provisioning Logic banata hai,
Agar native change already target system me ho gaya tha:-
AD me Finance group add ho gaya
aur Manager ne reject kar diya.
Toh method reverse plan banata hai:-
Finance group remove karo

4. ProvisioningPlan return karta hai:-
ProvisioningPlan object return karta hai resultVariable ke plan(plan Variable upar Workflow me defined hai) me.
*/////////
//////////*
()<Variable editable="true" initializer="false" name="optimisticProvisioning">
    <Description>
      Set to true to enable optimistic provisioning.  This will cause
      changes to the entitlements compiled from role assignments to be 
      applied immediately to the identity cube rather than waiting
      for the next refresh/reaggregation after the provisioning system
      completes the request.
    </Description>
  </Variable>:-
-->1. editable="true":-
Matlab:-
Workflow launch/change ke time is variable ki value modify ki ja sakti hai.

-->2. initializer="false" ye Default value false hai.
Matlab by default:-optimistic provisioning OFF hai.

-->4. name="optimisticProvisioning" Variable ka naam.

()Ab Main Concept:-Optimistic Provisioning kya hota hai?
Normally IIQ ka flow:-
Provisioning request gaya
        ↓
Target system update hua
        ↓
Aggregation/refresh hua
        ↓
Identity cube update hua

Isme delay hota hai.
Example:-
User ko AD group diya:-
Finance_Group
Provisioning request bheja gaya.

Lekin:-
identity cube tab tak update nahi hota jab tak:
aggregation
refresh
na chale.

Optimistic Provisioning ON
Agar:-
optimisticProvisioning = true
toh:
Provisioning request gaya
        ↓
IIQ maan lega ki success ho gaya
        ↓
Immediately identity cube update kar dega.

()initializer="false":-
Matlab agar kahi se value nahi aayi:-
optimisticProvisioning = false
rahega.

()ish <variable name="optimisticProvisioning"> me Value kaha se aa sakti hai?
1. Workflow launch arguments se
Workflow start karte time koi process value pass kar sakta hai.
Example:-
<Arg name="optimisticProvisioning" value="true"/>

()<Arg name="optimisticProvisioning" value="true"/> yaha value true set kiya gaya hai.
*//////////
///////////*
<Variable editable="true" initializer="true" name="foregroundProvisioning">
    <Description>
      Normally provisioning is done in a step that uses the "background"
      option to force the workflow to be suspend and be resumed in a
      background task thread.  This prevents the browser session from
      hanging since provision can sometimes take a long time.  For demos
      and testing it can be better to do this in the foreground so that
      provisioning will have been performed when control is returned to the
      user.  This prevents having to run the Perform Maintenance task to 
      see the results of the request.
    </Description>
  </Variable>
  
->>1.initializer="true":-
Default value:-
foregroundProvisioning = true

->>2.name="foregroundProvisioning":-
Variable name.

->>3. value kaha se aayega:-
(a).Workflow Argument se:-
Workflow launch karte time value pass ho sakti hai.
Example:-
<Arg name="foregroundProvisioning" value="false"/>
*/////////
/////////*
()Foreground vs Background Provisioning:-

()Foreground Provisioning:-
Workflow wait karega jab tak provisioning complete na ho
User ko response tab milega jab kaam finish ho jaye.

()Background Provisioning:-
Workflow suspend ho jayega
Provisioning alag thread/task me chalega
Browser free ho jata hai.
*////////

//////////*
()Workflow ke variable ki value kaha se milti hai batao:-
->
1. Parent Workflow se:-
Agar ye workflow kisi dusre workflow se call hua:
Parent workflow:-
<WorkflowRef>
ke through value pass kar sakta hai.
Example:-
<Arg name="foregroundProvisioning" value="true"/>

2. Script/Rule se:-
Workflow script me:-
foregroundProvisioning = false;
set ho sakta hai.

*/////////
//////////*
()1. Arg
Arg = Argument.
Ye:-
parameter pass karne ke liye use hota hai.

--jaise Java me method me parameter pass karte hai,
Java Example:-
myMethod(true);

--waise hi Workflow me aise pass karte hai value to variable:-
<Arg name="foregroundProvisioning" value="true"/>

2. name="foregroundProvisioning":-
Ye receiving side ka parameter/Variable name hai.
Receiving workflow/method me parameter/variable ka naam kya hoga.
Meaning:-
Receiver variable name:
foregroundProvisioning

3.value="true" pass hoga.

4.value="ref:foregroundProvisioning"/>:-
--.ref:-
Bahut important.
ref: ka matlab:-
Existing workflow variable ki actual value use karo.
--foregroundProvisioning:-Current workflow variable ka naam,Ye variable pehle declare hua tha.
matlab existing workflow ki value ko pass karo.

  </Variable>
:-

()<Arg name="trace" value="ref:trace"/>:-Current workflow ki existing value ko dusre workflow(LCM Provisioning)/method(buildApprovalSetFromNativeChanges(event);)
 ko PASS kar rahi hai.

Current workflow ke trace variable ki actual value ko dusre workflow/method me trace naam ke argument ke roop me pass karo.

()kis workflow me bhej raha hai mere diye gaye workflow me kaha kishi dusre workflow ka naam hai?
Haan, tumhare diye workflow me dusre workflow ka naam clearly diya hua hai.

<WorkflowRef>
  <Reference class="sailpoint.object.Workflow"
             name="LCM Provisioning"/>
</WorkflowRef>
Matlab:-
Current workflow:-
Lifecycle Event - Manager Approval for all native changes

dusra workflow call kar raha hai:-
LCM Provisioning

()<Variable initializer="Modify" name="operations">:-

()Ye line dekho:-
<Step name="Build Op String" resultVariable="operations">
Is step me:-
return Util.listToCsv(ops);
return ho raha hai.
Aur:-
resultVariable="operations"
matlab returned value:-
operations variable me save hogi.

<Step name="Build Op String" posX="81" posY="20" resultVariable="operations">
    <Script>
      <Source>
        import sailpoint.object.NativeChangeDetection;
        import sailpoint.object.ProvisioningPlan.AccountRequest;
        import sailpoint.tools.Util;
        
        List ops = new ArrayList();
        if ( event != null ) {
            List ncs = event.getNativeChanges();
            if ( ncs != null ) {
                for ( NativeChangeDetection nc : ncs ) {
                    AccountRequest.Operation op = nc.getOperation();
                    if ( op == null ) 
                        opString = "Modify";
                    else
                        opString = op.toString();

                    if ( !ops.contains(opString) ) {
                        ops.add(opString);
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        return Util.listToCsv(ops);
      </Source>
    </Script>
    <Transition to="Build Native Change Approval"/>
  </Step>

()1. Util.listToCsv(ops):-
Ye method:-
List ko CSV (Comma Separated String) me convert karta hai.
Example:-
List ops = ["Modify", "Delete"];

-><Step catches="complete" icon="Catches" name="Complete">
👉 Ye SailPoint workflow ka final “catch/cleanup step” hota hai.

->1. Identity Request finalize karta hai
👉 request ko “complete” state me lock karta hai

->2. Audit / logging trigger karta hai
👉 kya hua, kya approve/reject hua, sab record hota hai

->3. Final workflow call karta hai
Tumhare XML me:-
<WorkflowRef>
  Identity Request Finalize
</WorkflowRef>
👉 matlab:-
final cleanup process run hota hai

->4. WorkItem / Comments close karta hai
👉 pending work items ko finalize/close karta hai.

->>5.Finalize kya karta hai?
request ko Completed status deta hai
provisioning + approval ka final result save karta hai
audit log create karta hai (kisne kya approve/reject kiya)
Identity request ko properly close karta hai
saare data (project, approvalSet, requestId) ko system me lock karta hai.

->>project → Ye provisioning ka final output object hota hai, jisme saare account changes (create/update/delete, entitlements changes) ka complete result stored hota hai, jo aage audit aur finalize process me use hota hai.
->>trace → Ye debugging flag hota hai jo decide karta hai ki workflow execution ka detailed log print hoga ya nahi, jisse developer issues troubleshoot kar sakta hai.
->>approvalSet → Isme manager ke saare approval/rejection decisions store hote hain, jaise kis attribute ya access ko approve ya reject kiya gaya aur uske comments kya hain.
->>identityRequestId → Ye har request ka unique identifier hota hai jo system me tracking, audit trail aur future reference ke liye use hota hai.

()<Variable name="operations" input="true"></Variable>
Jab bhi yeh workflow chalega, toh isko chalane wala (Parent ya SailPoint) is box ke andar batayega ki kaun sa operation 
(jaise Enable, Disable, Modify) perform karna hai.
Aapka doosra sawal sabse important hai: Iske andar value SailPoint dega ya fir Parent dega?
Iska seedha jawaab hai: Dono de sakte hain.

()Case A: Identity Lifecycle Event se (Trigger):-
Maan lijiye aapne is workflow ko ek Termination Lifecycle Event ke sath map kiya hai. 
Jab SailPoint kisi user ka termination detect karega, toh SailPoint ka Lifecycle Engine background mein is workflow ko trigger karega.
Agar aapne Lifecycle Event setting mein koi static ya dynamic value pass ki hai, toh SailPoint use is variable mein fill kar dega.

()Case B: QuickLink ya LCM Form se:-
Maan lijiye aapne SailPoint UI mein ek custom form banaya hai jahan Manager dropdown se select karta hai: "Disable User".
Jab Manager form submit karega, toh SailPoint UI us selected value ko uthayega aur aapke workflow ke operations variable mein pass kar dega.

1. Kya yeh koi bhi value (Create, Modify, etc.) store kar sakta hai?
Haan, bilkul kar sakta hai. SailPoint mein workflow variables default roop se ek generic java.lang.String ya java.lang.Object ki tarah treat hote hain. Aap isme koi bhi text value store kar sakte hain.

Case A: Ek baar mein sirf EK value store karni ho (String format)
Agar aapka workflow ek baar mein sirf ek hi kaam karta hai (jaise sirf Disable ya sirf Enable), toh aap isme single text store karenge:

operations = "Create"

operations = "Disable"

Case B: Ek baar mein MULTIPLE values store karni hon (List format)
Agar aap chahte hain ki yeh ek se zyada values store kare (jaise ek sath Disable bhi kare aur Delete bhi), 
toh aapko is variable ka type java.util.List define karna padega.

XML mein yeh aisa dikhega:-
XML
<Variable name="operations" type="java.util.List" input="true" />
Ab Parent Workflow ya SailPoint isme ek sath multiple values bhej sakta hai: ["Modify", "Enable"].
*//////////
////////////*
()note:-ObjectOperation.Set/ObjectOperation.Add/ObjectOperation.Remove ye Enum Objects hai, 
yeh koi string variable nahi hai. Aap Enum class ke upar direct .equalsIgnoreCase() nahi chala sakte.

()NativeChangeDetection kya hai?
Jab target system par direct koi admin chhedkhani karta hai (bina SailPoint ke approval ke), 
toh use SailPoint ke andar Native Change bola jata hai. 
Aur is poore process ko track karne ke liye SailPoint ke paas ek built-in class aur process hoti hai jise NativeChangeDetection kehte hain.

1. Yeh Kab Aur Kaise Kaam Karta Hai?
Maan lijiye aapka Active Directory (AD) ka application SailPoint se connected hai.

--Direct Action: Kisi IT Helpdesk team ke member ne direct AD Users & Computers tool khola aur user Rahul ka department badal kar
"Sales" se "Marketing" kar diya.

--Aggregation Task: Raat ko jab SailPoint ka Account Aggregation task chala, 
toh woh AD se sabhi users ka current data utha kar laya.

--Detection: SailPoint ne dekha ki database mein Rahul ka department "Sales" tha, lekin AD se "Marketing" aa raha hai, 
aur yeh change SailPoint ke kisi Provisioning Plan se nahi hua hai.

--Triggering Lifecycle: Yahan par NativeChangeDetection engine active hota hai. 
Yeh ek IdentityChangeEvent generate karta hai aur usme event.getNativeChanges() ke andar is badlav ko store kar deta hai.

()2. Aggregation Task (Data ka SailPoint mein aana):-
Yeh kahan hota hai? Jab aapka Account Aggregation Task chalta hai, 
toh SailPoint ka Connector target system se saara raw data khinch kar lata hai.
Iska data kahan rehta hai? Yeh data temporary roop se ResourceObject class ke andar store hota hai. 
SailPoint is ResourceObject (jo AD se abhi-abhi aaya hai) ko user ke purane Link object 
(jo SailPoint ke database mein pehle se save tha) ke sath compare (match) karta hai.

import sailpoint.object.Link;
import sailpoint.object.ResourceObject;
import sailpoint.object.Identity;
import sailpoint.tools.Util;

// Maan lijiye yeh dono objects aapko rule ya task ke context se mil rahe hain
// Link link = ... (SailPoint ke database mein save purana account data)
// ResourceObject rObj = ... (AD se aggregation ke dauran aaya naya data)

if (link != null && rObj != null) {

    // 1. LINK OBJECT (Old Data from SailPoint DB)
    // Link ke andar se purana attribute nikalna
    String oldDepartment = (String) link.getAttribute("department");
    String oldTitle = (String) link.getAttribute("title");

    // 2. RESOURCE OBJECT (New Data coming from Active Directory)
    // ResourceObject ke andar se naya incoming attribute nikalna
    String newDepartment = (String) rObj.getAttribute("department");
    String newTitle = (String) rObj.getAttribute("title");

    System.out.println("--- Comparing Link (Old) vs ResourceObject (New AD Data) ---");

    // -------------------------------------------------------------------------
    // Scenario 1: Department Compare Karna
    // -------------------------------------------------------------------------
    // Util.nullSafeEquality use karna best practice hai taaki null hone par crash na ho
    if (!Util.nullSafeEquality(oldDepartment, newDepartment)) {
        
        System.out.println("ALERT: Department badal gaya hai!");
        System.out.println("Old Data (Link DB): " + oldDepartment);
        System.out.println("New Data (ResourceObject AD): " + newDepartment);
        
        // Aap yahan apna custom logic likh sakte hain
    } else {
        System.out.println("Department mein koi badlav nahi hai.");
    }

    // -------------------------------------------------------------------------
    // Scenario 2: Job Title Compare Karna
    // -------------------------------------------------------------------------
    if (!Util.nullSafeEquality(oldTitle, newTitle)) {
        
        System.out.println("ALERT: Job Title badal gaya hai!");
        System.out.println("Old Data (Link DB): " + oldTitle);
        System.out.println("New Data (ResourceObject AD): " + newTitle);
        
    } else {
        System.out.println("Job Title mein koi badlav nahi hai.");
    }
}
*///////////
/////////////*
()1.renderer="nativeChangeApprovalRenderer.xhtml" toh Yeh Line Karti Kya Hai?
SailPoint me jab koi manager ya approver apna Inbox / Dashboard kholta hai, toh use approvals ki list dikhti hai.
Lekin har approval ek jaisa nahi hota (kuch normal access requests hoti hain, toh kuch native changes hote hain). 
renderer attribute SailPoint ko batata hai ki is specific approval set ko screen par dikhane ke liye kis UI template ya design ka use karna hai.
nativeChangeApprovalRenderer.xhtml ek pre-defined JSF (JavaServer Faces) page hai.
Yeh page manager ke saamne ek specific layout kholta hai jo native changes ke liye hi design kiya gaya hai.

2. Manager ko Screen Par Kya Dikhega?
Jab yeh renderer load hoga, toh approver ko screen par kuch is tarah ka data saaf-saaf dikhega:-
Field                         Description
Identity / User-----------Kis employee ke account me badlav hua hai.
Application-----Kis target system (jaise Active Directory, SAP) me change hua.
Native Change---Exact kya change hua (e.g., "Added to Domain Admins Group").
Action Buttons--Approve (is change ko valid maano) ya Reject/Remediate (is change ko rollback karo).
*//////////
/////////////*
()<Approval mode="parallel" owner="script:getManagerName(identityName, launcher, fallbackApprover);" 
	renderer="nativeChangeApprovalRenderer.xhtml" send="identityDisplayName,identityName">
script:getManagerName(identityName, launcher, fallbackApprover);:-
1. Teeno Parameters Ka Kya Kaam Hai?
जब SailPoint yeh script chalayega, toh woh in teen cheezon ko check karega:-
-->identityName: Yeh us employee/user ki Identity hai jiske account me native change hua hai. 
Script sabse pehle is user ke profile (Identity Cube) par jaakar iske manager ka naam dhoodhne ki koshish karegi.

-->launcher: Yeh us user ki Identity hai jisme is workflow ko start (launch) kiya. 
Kyunki yeh native change hai (jo background aggregation se pakda gaya hai), toh aksar launcher spadmin ya System hota hai.

-->fallbackApprover: Yeh aapka Backup Plan (Safety Net) hai.Agar kisi wajah se target user ka koi manager assigned nahi hai 
(jaise CEO ka koi manager nahi hota, ya HR data me manager missing hai), 
toh approval request hawa me na ghumne ki jagah is default fallbackApprover (jaise ki Compliance Team ya System Administrator) ke paas chali jayegi.
*/////////

/////////////*
<Script> (Data Loader / Value Script)
Kaam kya hai: Iska kaam field ke andar data ko load ya populate karna hota hai.
Ye batata hai ki us box me user ko kya dikhega.
ex:-
1. <Script> Ka Kaam (Step ke Shuru me):-
Yeh step ke shuru hote hi chalta hai taaki approval ke liye taiyari ki ja sake.
XML
<Script>
  // Step shuru hone se pehle manager ka naam dhoodho
  String manager = getManagerName(identityName, launcher, "Default Workgroup");
  workflow.put("approverName", manager); 
</Script>

2. <AfterScript> Ka Kaam (Step Khatam hone ke Baad):
Ab manager ne screen par "Approve" ya "Reject" button daba diya aur step khatam ho gaya. 
ex:-
Ab <AfterScript> trigger hoga yeh dekhne ke liye ki manager ne kya faisla liya:-
XML
<AfterScript>
  // Step khatam hone ke baad check karo manager ne kya kiya
  String decision = item.getApprovalState(); // Approve ya Reject check karna
  log.error("Manager ka decision tha: " + decision);
  
  if("Rejected".equals(decision)) {
      // Agar reject kiya toh koi alert trigger karo
      sendAlertToSecurityTeam(identityName);
  }
</AfterScript>

3. <ValidationScript> (Data Checker / Guard):-
Kaam kya hai: Iska kaam user ke bhare hue data ko check (verify) karna hota hai ki wo sahi hai ya galat.
Kab chalta hai: Jab user form poora bharne ke baad "Save" ya "Next" button daba kar submit karta hai. 
Return Type: * Agar data galat hai, to ye ek Error Message (String) return karta hai 
(jo screen par red color me dikhta hai aur workflow ko aage badhne se rok deta hai).
Agar data sahi hai, to ye null ya kuch return nahi karta, jisse workflow aage badh jata hai.

toh yeh script check karti hai ki jo data submit kiya ja raha hai, woh sahi hai ya nahi.
1. Yeh Kab Aur Kaise Chalta Hai?
Jab workflow kisi Form ya Approval step par ruka hota hai aur user button click karta hai, 
toh SailPoint agle step par jaane se pehle <ValidationScript> ko chalata hai.
ex:-
2. Ek Real-World Example Se Samjhein:-
Maan lijiye aapke native change approval workflow me aapne manager ko ek text box diya hai jisme use likhna hai: "Aap is native change ko kyun approve kar rahe hain? (Reason)"
Aap chahte hain ki manager bina reason likhe "Approve" na kar paye. Wahan aap <ValidationScript> ka use karenge:
XML
<ValidationScript>
  <Source>
    // Manager ne jo comments likhe hain use nikalye
    String comments = item.getComments(); 
    
    // Agar comments khali hain ya bohot chhote hain
    if (comments == null || comments.trim().length() &lt; 10) {
        // Form rok do aur screen par error dikhao
        return "Error: Native change ko approve karne ke liye kam se kam 10 characters ka reason likhna zaroori hai!";
    }
    
    return null; // Sab sahi hai, aage badhne do
  </Source>
</ValidationScript>
*///////////////////
//////////*
()launcher kaise nikale?
launcher me value SailPoint khud automatic tarike se daal kar deta hai. Aapko isse alag se define karne ki ya isme koi value manually bharne ki zaroorat nahi hoti.
Direct Variable: SailPoint workflows me launcher naam ka variable pehle se implicit (built-in) hota hai. 
Aap direct launcher use kar sakte hain.

Context Se Nikalna: Agar aapko script ke andar nikalna hai, 
toh aap workflow.getLauncher() ya wfcontext.getWorkflow().getLauncher() ka use karte hain.
*/////////////
////////////////*
pehle variable ko declare karte hai:-<Variable name="launcher" input="true"></Variable>
fir value kahi bhi koi bhi step me dalkar ush variable ko use karte hai:-<Arg name="workItemRequester" value="$(launcher)"/>
*///////////////
//note:-ApprovalSet jishme sare approvals/items bante hai wo ApprovalSet ke approver ko send hone ke baad hi WorkItem bante hai.

//////*
note:-Galti yeh hai ki item.getApprovalSet() aapko koi text (String) return nahi karta, 
balki yeh pura ka pura ApprovalSet Object return karta hai (jisme saare native changes aur attributes ki details hoti hain).
Ek poore object ko aap direct "Approve" text ke sath .equals() se compare nahi kar sakte.
ex:-script:item.getApprovalSet().equals(&quot;Approve&quot;)-->ye galat hai.-----------------galat hai ye line.
Script: &quot;Approved&quot;.equals(item.getApprovalState())-->sahi ye hai.
Script: item.getApprovalSet() != null &amp;&amp; item.getApprovalSet().isApproved()-->sahi ye hai.
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
()when="script:item.getApprovalState().equals(&quot;Approved&quot;)" ye sahi hai ki nahi,
ye kaam karega lekin crash bhi ho jayega.
--->Isme Risk Kya Hai?
Aapne likha hai: item.getApprovalState().equals("Approved")

Maan lijiye kisi wajah se us approval item ka state abhi update nahi hua hai, 
ya woh null (khali) hai. Aise me jab system null.equals("Approved") karne ki koshish karega, 
toh workflow wahi par crash ho jayega (NullPointerException dega) aur aapka poora task ruk jayega.

Iska 100% Sahi aur Safe Version Kya Hai?
Java aur BeanShell me isse bachne ka ek universal rule hai—hamesha fixed text ("Approved") ko pehle likho, aur variable ko .equals() ke andar daalo.

Aap isse badalkar aise likhiye:-
XML
when="Script: &quot;Approved&quot;.equals(item.getApprovalState())"

Java aur SailPoint (BeanShell) me yeh ek bohot bada niyam (rule) hai: Aap kisi poore Object (jaise ApprovalSet) ko
ek simple text (String jaise "Approve") se seedhe compare nahi kar sakte.
Agar aap aisa karenge, toh dono ka data type alag hone ki wajah se result hamesha false aayega ya fir code crash ho jayega.
*/////
/////////*
()resolveDisplayName() SailPoint IdentityIQ (IIQ) ka ek bohot hi useful utility method hai, 
jo aamtaor par sailpoint.object.Identity class ya SailPoint ki internal API classes (jaise sailpoint.api.ObjectUtil) ka hissa
hota hai.
resolveDisplayName thik yahi kaam karta hai:-
Aap is method ko koi Identity Name (ID) dete hain.
Yeh database me jaakar us Identity ka displayName dhoodhta hai (jaise: First Name + Last Name).
Agar user ka display name set hai, toh yeh use return kar dega (e.g., "Rahul Sharma").
Backup Plan: Agar kisi user ka display name set nahi hai (null hai), toh yeh workflow ko crash nahi karta, 
balki backup me uska Unique Username/ID hi return kar deta hai taaki screen khali na dikhe.
*/////////
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
//////////////*
()semicolon(;):-
kyunki SailPoint me semicolon (;) lagana hai ya nahi, 
yeh is baat par depend karta hai ki aap script ko XML ke kis attribute ya tag ke andar likh rahe hain.

-->Rule 1: Agar aap <Transition> tag ke andar hain (Semicolon NAHI lagana hai)
Jab aap kisi step se dusre step par jaane ke liye single-line condition likhte hain (jaise when="Script:..."), toh wahan semicolon nahi lagaya jata.
Kyun? Kyunki SailPoint wahan ek "Expression" expect karta hai jo turant true ya false (ya koi value) return kare. Semicolon lagane se BeanShell use ek statement maan leta hai aur kabhi-kabhi kuch return nahi karta (void ho jata hai), jisse workflow ruk jata hai.
❌ Galat: when="Script: "Approved".equals(item.getApprovalState());"
Sahi: when="Script: "Approved".equals(item.getApprovalState())"

Rule 2: Agar aap <Source> ya <Script> tag ke andar hain (Semicolon ZAROORI hai).

Rule 3:-
Agar aap <Approval> tag ke attributes jaise ownerExpression, argIdentity, ya when ke andar script: prefix ke sath single-line expression likh rahe hain, toh wahan semicolon nahi lagana hai.

Kyun? Kyunki SailPoint yahan direct ek dynamic value ya object return chahta hai. Semicolon lagane se logic break ho sakta hai.

❌ Galat:

XML
<Approval name="Manager Approval" ownerExpression="script:getManagerName(identityName, launcher, fallbackApprover);" renderer="nativeChangeApprovalRenderer.xhtml">
*   ✅ **Sahi:**
    ```xml
    <Approval name="Manager Approval" ownerExpression="script:getManagerName(identityName, launcher, fallbackApprover)" renderer="nativeChangeApprovalRenderer.xhtml">
Scenario 2: Agar aap Approval ke andar <Script> ya <ValidationScript> block bana rahe hain (Semicolon HAMESHA lagega)
*///////////
///////////////*
()provisionRejectedItems SailPoint IdentityIQ (IIQ) ke workflows me ek bohot hi important Configuration Variable (Setting) hai.
Aasan bhasha me samjhein toh yeh ek Switch (On/Off Button) ki tarah hai,
jo SailPoint ko yeh batata hai ki: "Agar manager ne kisi request ya change ko 'Reject' kar diya hai, 
toh kya SailPoint ko target system me jaakar us access ko sach me delete/remediate karna hai ya nahi?"
true hone pe karta hai aur fale hone pe nahi karega deprovision/remediation.
-->value koun deta hai:-
provisionRejectedItems variable ki value SailPoint khud automatic tarike se deta hai(uski default settings se), 
lekin developers ya administrators iski value ko manually badal (override) bhi sakte hain.
*////////////
()<Arg name="flow" value="EntitlementsRequest"/>called pipeline(jisse bhi call kar rahe chahe action="method"/workflow) ko bata rahe hai ki
value="EntitlementsRequest":matlab Yeh batata hai ki is workflow trigger ka main maqsad kya hai.Yahan iska maqsad hai kisi user ke liye kisi specific target system (jaise Active Directory) ke Entitlement (Group, Role, ya Attribute) ko request karna.

<?xml version='1.0' encoding='UTF-8'?>
<!DOCTYPE sailpoint PUBLIC "sailpoint.dtd" "sailpoint.dtd">
<sailpoint>
<Workflow explicitTransitions="true" name="Approve and Provision Subprocess" type="Subprocess">
  <Variable input="true" name="identityName">
    <Description>The name of the identity being updated.</Description>
  </Variable>
  <Variable initializer="false" input="true" name="endOnManualWorkItems">
    <Description>Option to skip requests with manual work items.</Description>
  </Variable>
  <Variable initializer="false" input="true" name="endOnProvisioningForms">
    <Description>Option to skip requests with provisioning forms.</Description>
  </Variable>
  <Variable initializer="script:(identityDisplayName != void) ? identityDisplayName : resolveDisplayName(identityName)" input="true" name="identityDisplayName">
    <Description>
            The displayName of the identity being updated.
            Query for this using a projection query and fall back to the name.
        </Description>
  </Variable>
  <Variable input="true" name="plan">
    <Description>The provisioning plan ready to execute.</Description>
  </Variable>
  <Variable input="true" name="flow">
    <Description>
            The name of the LCM flow that launched this workflow.

            This is one of these three values:

            AccountsRequest
            EntitlementsRequest
            RolesRequest
        </Description>
  </Variable>
  <Variable editable="true" initializer="false" name="optimisticProvisioning">
    <Description>
            Set to true to enable optimistic provisioning.  This will cause
            changes to the entitlements compiled from role assignments to be
            applied immediately to the identity cube rather than waiting
            for the next refresh/reaggregation after the provisioning system
            completes the request.
        </Description>
  </Variable>
  <Variable editable="true" initializer="true" name="foregroundProvisioning">
    <Description>
            Normally provisioning is done in a step that uses the "background"
            option to force the workflow to be suspend and be resumed in a
            background task thread.  This prevents the browser session from
            hanging since provision can sometimes take a long time.  For demos
            and testing it can be better to do this in the foreground so that
            provisioning will have been performed when control is returned to the
            user.  This prevents having to run the Perform Maintenance task to
            see the results of the request.
        </Description>
  </Variable>
  <Variable input="true" name="batchRequestItemId">
    <Description>
            Used by the batch interface to record back individual request item status. The specific item id for the individual request in the batch file.
        </Description>
  </Variable>
  <Variable initializer="LCM User Notification" input="true" name="userEmailTemplate">
    <Description>
            The email template to use for user notification.
        </Description>
  </Variable>
  <Variable initializer="LCM Requester Notification" input="true" name="requesterEmailTemplate">
    <Description>
            The email template to use for requester notification.
        </Description>
  </Variable>
  <Variable initializer="LCM Manager Notification" input="true" name="managerEmailTemplate">
    <Description>
            The email template to use for manager notification.
        </Description>
  </Variable>
  <Variable input="true" name="securityOfficerEmailTemplate">
    <Description>
            The email template to use for security officer notification.
        </Description>
  </Variable>
  <Variable initializer="parallel" input="true" name="approvalMode">
    <Description>
            A string that specifies how we should handle the approvals.

            By default this is serial since most of these request with
            the exception of manager transfers will have only one approver.

            parallel
            Approvals are processed concurrently and there must be consensus,
            we wait for all approvers to approve.  The first approver that
            rejects terminates the entire approval.

            parallelPoll
            Approvals are processed concurrently but consensus is not required.
            All approvals will be processed, we don't stop if there are any
            rejections.

            serial
            Approvals are processed one at a time and there must be consensus.
            The first approver that rejects terminates the entire approval.

            serialPoll
            Approvals are processed in order but consensus is not required.
            All approvals will be processed, we don't stop if there are any
            rejections.  In effect we are "taking a poll" of the approvers.

            any
            Approvals are processed concurrently, the first approver to
            respond makes the decision for the group.
        </Description>
  </Variable>
  <Variable initializer="owner" input="true" name="approvalScheme">
    <Description>
            A csv string that specifies how approval items should be generated
            for the incoming request.

            The value can be "none", in which case approvals are disabled.

            The value can also be a combination of any of the values below
            in any order, separated by commas. The order in which they are
            specified is the order in which they are processed:

            owner
            The object owner gets the approval item.
            For Role approvals this is the Role object owner.
            For Entitlement approvals this is the Entitlement object owner.

            manager
            The manager gets the approval item.

            securityOfficer
            The identity in the variable securityOfficerName gets the approval item.

            identity
            The identities/workgroups in the variable approvingIdentities get the approval item.
        </Description>
  </Variable>
  <Variable initializer="LCM Identity Update Approval" input="true" name="approvalEmailTemplate">
    <Description>
            The email template to use for approval notifications.
        </Description>
  </Variable>
  <Variable initializer="Normal" input="true" name="workItemPriority">
    <Description>
            The String version of a WorkItem.Priority. This variable is
            used to set the priority on all of the workitems generated
            as part of this workflow and also set on the IdentityRequest
            object.
        </Description>
  </Variable>
  <Variable input="true" name="securityOfficerName">
    <Description>
            The name of the identity that will be sent approvals
            during security officer approvals.
        </Description>
  </Variable>
  <Variable initializer="spadmin" input="true" name="fallbackApprover">
    <Description>
            A String that specifies the name of the Identity that will
            be assigned any approvals where the owner of the approver
            can't be resolved. Example if the scheme is "owner" and the
            application doesn't specify and owner.
        </Description>
  </Variable>
  <Variable initializer="false" input="true" name="enableRetryRequest">
    <Description>
            When set to true it will disable the workflow retry loop and let the
            Provision step launch requests to handle the retries.  Enabling
            this flag will enable some older functionality.
        </Description>
  </Variable>
  <Variable initializer="LCM" input="true" name="source">
    <Description>
            String version of sailpoint.object.Source to indicate
            where the request originated.  Defaults to LCM.
        </Description>
  </Variable>
  <Variable initializer="false" name="trace">
    <Description>
            Used for debugging this workflow and when set to true trace
            will be sent to stdout.
        </Description>
  </Variable>
  <Variable name="approvalSet">
    <Description>
            This attributes is set during the "Build Approval Set" step,
            which builds this list by going through the ProvisioningPlan
            to build the line items that need to be approved,

            This variable includes all ApprovalItems that are part of
            the request process and is updated during the AfterScript
            of the approval process by assimilating the decisions
            and comments from the Approvals copy of the ApprovalItem.
        </Description>
  </Variable>
  <Variable input="true" name="approvalAssignmentRule"/>
  <Variable name="project">
    <Description>
            ProvisioningProject which is just a compiled version of the ProvisioningPlan.
        </Description>
  </Variable>
  <Variable name="policyViolations">
    <Description>
            List of policy violations that were found during our initial policy scan.
            This list is passed into each work item so the approvers can see
            pending violations.
        </Description>
  </Variable>
  <Variable name="identityRequestId" output="true">
    <Description>
            The sequence id of the Identity request object which is stored in
            the name field of the identity request and auto-incremented.
        </Description>
  </Variable>
  <Variable name="workItemComments">
    <Description>
            Global comments accumulated during the workflow which should be shared
            with other approvals. When a new approval is created, the comments in this
            list will be added to the work item.
        </Description>
  </Variable>
  <Variable input="true" name="ticketManagementApplication">
    <Description>
            Name of the application that can handle ticket requests.
            When non-null the Manage Ticket Steps will be visited to open
            tickets during the workflow lifecycle.
        </Description>
  </Variable>
  <Variable input="true" name="managerElectronicSignature">
    <Description>
            The name of the electronic signature object that should be used when workitems
            are completed by a manager.
        </Description>
  </Variable>
  <Variable input="true" name="ownerElectronicSignature">
    <Description>
            The name of the electronic signature object that should be used when workitems
            are completed by object owners.
        </Description>
  </Variable>
  <Variable input="true" name="securityOfficerElectronicSignature">
    <Description>
            The name of the electronic signature object that should be used when workitems
            are completed by the security officer.
        </Description>
  </Variable>
  <Variable initializer="true" input="true" name="filterRejects">
    <Description>True to filter rejected items when running in Serial/SerialPoll mode.</Description>
  </Variable>
  <Variable initializer="false" input="true" name="setPreviousApprovalDecisions">
    <Description>True to pre-populate approval decisions from previous approvals.</Description>
  </Variable>

  </Variable>

        </Description>
  </Variable>

        </Description>
  </Variable>
  <Variable input="true" name="formTemplate"/>

            Name of the email template to use when notifying the owner of pending approvals.
        </Description>
  </Variable>
  <Variable initializer="false" input="true" name="splitProvisioning">
    <Description>
            True to tell IdentityRequest Provisioning subprocess that this is a subset of the initial provisioning plan
        </Description>
  </Variable>
  <Description>Subprocess to approve and provision immediately. This is used after splitting an ApprovalSet into individual items to run in parallel.</Description>

  </RuleLibraries>

                    if ("ForgotPassword".equals(flow) || "ExpirePassword".equals(flow)) {

    <Arg name="identityDisplayName" value="ref:identityDisplayName"/>

    <Arg name="identityEmailTemplate"/>

/////////////*
()flow me kitne tarah ke value aa sakte hai?non custom workflow me flow ki value ek baar hi shuru me set hoti hai.
-->flow variable ko value sailpoint deta hai,aur ye workflow ka flow batata hai ye workflow kya karega ya kis kaam ke liye ishko trigger kiya gaya hai.
note:-getVariable(flow) mein galti:-
Variable ka naam hamesha double quotes mein string ki tarah pass hota hai, 
jaise: getVariable("flow"). Agar aap bina quotes ke flow likhoge, toh system confuse ho jayega.

1. Lifecycle Events:-
Jab company mein kisi employee ka status badalta hai, toh SailPoint automatic ek flow trigger karta hai. 
Us waqt flow ya event.getName() mein niche di gayi values aati hain:-
-->Joiner / IdentityLifecycle-Joiner: Jab koi naya employee company join karta hai aur uska naya account banta hai.
-->Mover / IdentityLifecycle-Mover: Jab kisi employee ka department, manager, ya location badalti hai (Transfer hota hai).
-->Leaver / IdentityLifecycle-Leaver / Termination: Jab koi employee company chhodta hai aur uske saare accounts disable kiye jaate hain.
-->Rehire: Jab koi purana employee dobara company join karta hai.

2. Access Requests (Lifecycle ke alawa manual requests):-
Agar koi user ya manager SailPoint portal par jaakar manually kuch request karta hai, 
toh flow ya quickAction ke andar yeh values aati hain:
-->AccessRequest / provideAccess: Jab kisi user ke liye koi naya Role ya Entitlement request kiya jata hai.
-->IdentityUpdate: Jab user ki profile identity details (jaise phone number, secondary email) update hoti hain.
-->ForgotPassword / PasswordReset: Jab koi user apna password bhool jata hai aur use reset karne ki request daalta hai.
-->AccountAggregation: Jab system background mein kisi application (jaise Active Directory ya HR system) se data khinch raha hota hai.

3. Certification & Compliance Flows:-
Jab audit chal raha ho ya access review ho raha ho, tab workflows mein alag tarah ki values aati hain:-
-->Certification: Jab managers ko apne employees ki access review karni hoti hai ki access sahi hai ya nahi.
-->Remediation: Agar audit ke waqt manager kisi access ko Revoke (hataane) ka faisla karta hai,toh access delete karne ke liye yeh flow chalta hai.
-->PolicyViolation: Agar koi user Sod (Segregation of Duties) policy todta hai (jaise ek hi bande ke paas Invoice Create aur Invoice Approve dono ki access ho), toh alert generate karne ke liye yeh flow trigger hota hai.
*//////////
///////////*
()<Arg name="noApplicationTemplates">:-SailPoint IdentityIQ ke standard workflows(jaise LCM Provisioning ya Subprocess workflows) 
mein use hone wala ek bahut hi important Argument (System Parameter) hai.
noApplicationTemplates Kya Kaam Karta Hai?
Jab yeh argument true hota hai, toh yeh SailPoint ko order deta hai ki:-
"Provisioning ke time par jo bhi standard Application Forms, Provisioning Policies, ya Multi-instance Account Templates hote hain, 
unhe skip kar do. User ya Manager ke samne koi pop-up form mat dikhao."Agar yeh false hota hai, 
toh SailPoint normal tarike se application ka form screen par dikhata hai taaki required fields 
(jaise target directory path, access levels) bhari ja sakein.
ex:-
Real-World Use Case (Yeh kyun zaroori hai?)
Aapne pichle code mein dekha ki yeh ForgotPassword aur ExpirePassword ke liye true ho raha tha.Iska bada reason yeh hai:-
-->Scenario A (Normal Access Request - noApplicationTemplates = false):-Maano aap kisi user ko Active Directory (AD) ki access 
de rahe ho. SailPoint beech mein rukega aur ek Form dikhayega:"Bhai, is user ka OU (Organizational Unit) select karo, 
ya iska mailbox size batao." Yahan form zaroori hai.

-->Scenario B (Password Reset - noApplicationTemplates = true):-Wahi user apna AD password bhool gaya aur ForgotPassword par 
click kiya. Ab SailPoint ko sirf password update karna hai,
use naya account thodi banana hai! Agar is time par bhi SailPoint beech mein wahi purana AD Form khol kar baith jaye 
(ki OU batao, department batao), toh user pareshan ho jayega.
Isliye Password Reset ke waqt noApplicationTemplates ko true pass kar diya jata hai taaki workflow bina kisi rukawat ya form-popup
ke chupchaap background mein password change kar de.
*///////////
////////////*
1.approvalSplitPoint variable ka Asli Kaam Kya Hai?
Maano ki aapne ek saath 3 applications ke liye access request daali: Active Directory (AD), SAP, aur Salesforce.
Ab in teeno applications ke approvals alag-alag logon ke paas jaane hain (jaise AD ka approval IT Team degi, SAP ka Finance Manager dega, aur Salesforce ka Sales Head dega).
approvalSplitPoint isi jagah par kaam aata hai:-
-->Plan ko Split Karna (Todna): Yeh chal rahe main Provisioning Plan ko dekhta hai aur use applications ya approvers ke hisab se alag-alag tukdon (sub-plans) mein tod deta hai.
-->Parallel Approvals Bhejna: Yeh teeno approvals ko ek saath (parallelly) unke respective managers ke paas bhej deta hai taaki kisi ek ke chakkar mein poora kaam na ruke.
-->Result ko Merge Karna: Jab teeno managers apna-apna approval de dete hain, toh approvalSplitPoint un saare approved tukdon ko wapas ek sath merge (jod) kar deta hai aur unhe aage final provisioning ke liye bhejta hai.

Plan Kaun Banata Hai? Workflow ka starting step (jaise Compile Project ya provisioning subprocess).
approvalSplitPoint Kya Karta Hai? Bane-banaye plan ko pakadta hai, use approval ke liye alag-alag hisson mein split (divide) karta hai, 
aur approvals milne ke baad wapas combine (merge) kar deta hai.

2.value koun deta hai approvalSplitPoint ko?
-->SailPoint ki Global Configuration (LCM Configuration) se
SailPoint ke UI mein ek jagah hoti hai jise LCM Configuration (Lifecycle Manager Configuration) kehte hain.
Wahan system administrator select karta hai ki approvals ka level kya hona chahiye:-
Approve by Application: Har application ke liye alag approval jaye.
Approve by Role: Har role ke liye alag approval jaye.
Jo bhi option UI mein select kiya jata hai, 
SailPoint background mein approvalSplitPoint variable ko wahi value (jaise "Application" ya "Role") de deta hai.
Bhai, aapne bilkul sahi pakda hai! approvalSplitPoint ke andar jo value hoti hai, 
woh asal mein ek list (ya scheme) hi hoti hai jo SailPoint ko batati hai ki pure plan ko kis basis par alag-alag tukdon mein todna hai.

()plan ka hissa hai approvalset?
Aapne jo kaha: "approvalSet toh plan ka tukda hai" — iska concept ekdum sahi hai, 
kyunki jo cheez approve honi hai, woh aakhirkaar plan se hi aayi hai.
Aaiye ab isko technical tarike se samajhte hain ki approvalSplitPoint dono ko kaise todta hai:-
-->Asliyat mein kya hota hai?
approvalSplitPoint sirf plan ko nahi todta, balki Plan aur ApprovalSet dono ko aamne-saamne rakh kar, 
ek saath(parallelly) unke jode (pairs) banakar todta hai.

()ProvisioningPlan (The "What" - Kya kaam hona hai): Identity: Amit ──> AccountRequest (Application: AD) ──> 
->AttributeRequest (Operation: Add, Name: memberOf, Value: Finance-Group).
(Yeh ekdum raw technical instruction hai engine ke liye).

()ApprovalSet (The "Who" - Kiski permission chahiye): ApprovalItem (Application: AD, Instance: Finance-Group, 
Approver: Rahul Manager, Status: Pending).
(Yeh sirf approvals ko track karne ke liye hai).

()1. Splitting se pehle (Bada Project):-
Bada ProvisioningPlan: [AD Request + SAP Request]
Bada ApprovalSet: [AD ApprovalItem (Manager) + SAP ApprovalItem (App Owner)]

2. approvalSplitPoint ka Action (The Breakdown):-
Yeh engine donon ko aapas mein match karta hai aur unke tukde kar deta hai:-
Tukda 1 (For AD): Isme se AD ka ProvisioningPlan aur AD ka ApprovalItem alag ho jata hai. 
Yeh dono milkar ek chota subprocess banate hain aur AD ke manager ke paas chale jaate hain.

Tukda 2 (For SAP): Isme se SAP ka ProvisioningPlan aur SAP ka ApprovalItem alag ho jata hai. 
Yeh dono milkar doosre subprocess mein SAP ke owner ke paas chale jaate hain.

flow:-
[User Request / Lifecycle Event] 
       │
       ▼
 1. Provisioning Plan (Pehle banta hai)
       │  (Sirf kacha data: "Amit ko Active Directory me Finance Group de do")
       ▼
 2. Compile Project (Workflow Step)
       │  (Is raw plan ko system compile karta hai)
       ▼
 3. Provisioning Project (Baad me banta hai)
       │  (Isme Plan + ApprovalSet dono taiyar hokar aate hain)
       ▼
 4. approvalSplitPoint:-plan ko todta hai approvalset ke samne,subset ban gaya(har subset ka workitem)
fir approver ke pass request jata hai aur approve/reject hone ke baad ye approvalSplitPoint unhe merge kar deta hai aur project me de deta hai.
*////////////
///////////////*
()<Step condition="script:((flow == null) ||  (!&quot;UnlockAccount&quot;.equals(flow)))" 
configForm="Provisioning Approval Step Form" icon="Approval" name="Approve" posX="320" posY="20">
 
-->flow == null: Agar flow ki koi value nahi hai (matlab normal ad-hoc request hai), toh approval step chalega.

-->!"UnlockAccount".equals(flow): Agar flow ki value UnlockAccount nahi hai (jaise Joiner, Mover, ya normal Access Request hai), toh bhi approval step chalega.

-->Iska ulti baat (Exception): Agar koi user apna account lock ho jaane par use Unlock kar raha hai (flow == "UnlockAccount"),
toh yeh condition false ho jayegi aur yeh approval step skip (bypass) ho jayega.
(Business reason: Account unlock karne ke liye kisi manager ke approval ka wait nahi kiya jata,use turant access chahiye hoti hai).

2. configForm="Provisioning Approval Step Form":-
Jab yeh step chalega aur manager ke paas approval jayega, toh manager ko screen par ek form dikhega.
Woh form kaisa dikhega, usme kaunse fields honge (jaise user ka naam, application ka naam, approve/reject ka button)
—yeh sab Provisioning Approval Step Form naam ke predefined form configuration se design hota hai.
*//////////////
////////////////*
()clearApprovalDecisions variable kya karta hai?
Iska Asli Kaam Kya Hai? (Business Use Case)
Maano ek bada access request chal raha tha jisme AD aur SAP dono maange gaye the.

Pehle step mein main Manager ne dono ko approve kar diya.

Uske baad plan split hua (approvalSplitPoint chala) aur AD chala gaya IT Team ke paas, 
aur SAP chala gaya Finance Team ke paas.

Maano Finance Team ne SAP ko Reject kar diya ya usme koi badlav kar diya, 
jiske wajah se request ko wapas pichle loop par aana pada.

Jab yeh cycle dobara ghum kar aayega, toh SailPoint is script ko chalayega.Agar yeh condition true return karti hai, 
toh SailPoint purane saare decisions ko reset (clear) kar dega taaki naye sire se approvals liye ja sakein aur koi purana decision 
automatic apply na ho jaye.

()<Arg name="clearApprovalDecisions" value="script:(!isNull(approvalSplitPoint) &amp;&amp; csvToList(approvalScheme).contains(approvalSplitPoint))"/>:-
1. !isNull(approvalSplitPoint):-
isNull(approvalSplitPoint) check karta hai ki kya split point khali hai.
Aage laga ! (NOT operator) isko ulta kar deta hai.
To iska matlab hua: "approvalSplitPoint khali nahi hona chahiye". 
Matlab system mein plan ko todne (split karne) ka logic active hai (jaise Application ya Role level par split ho raha hai).

2. csvToList(approvalScheme)approvalScheme ek workflow variable hota hai jisme comma-separated values (CSV) hoti hain, 
jaise: "manager,owner,security". Yeh batata hai ki approval kitne levels par hona hai.
csvToList(...) ek SailPoint ka in-built function hai jo is text ko ek proper Java List["manager", "owner", "security"] mein badal deta hai taaki system isme search kar sake.

3. .contains(approvalSplitPoint):-
Yeh check karta hai ki jo hamari current approvalSplitPoint ki value hai (jaise maano iski value "owner" hai), 
kya woh upar wali approvalScheme list ke andar maujood (contains) hai ya nahi?
