//////////*
note:-Agar variable identity null hai, toh uske upar koi bhi method chalana (jaise .getName(), .getAttribute(), etc.)  toh system NullPointerException dega bhai.
Java/Beanshell ka seedha niyam hai: "No Object, No Method." Agar object/variable null hai, toh object/variable pe koi bhi action perform karne par system turant haath khade kar dega aur NullPointerException (NPE) fekh ke maarega.

note:-1. Java ka "Single Line" Rule:-Java mein agar tum if ke baad { } nahi lagate, 
toh if condition sirf aur sirf uske theek neeche wali EK LINE par apply hoti hai. 
Uske baad ki saari lines aam code ki tarah chalti hain, chahe if sahi ho ya galat.
agar agla code line ka variable null hai aur chali toh NullPointerException milega.

note:-if(idn != null):-
String identityName = idn.getName(); // 💥 SYNTAX ERROR!
Java ka ek bohot strict rule hai: Aap bina curly braces { } ke kisi if statement ke theek baad naya variable declare (create) nahi kar sakte. Aisa kyun?
Java sochta hai ki agar tumne naya variable banaya hai, toh tum use aage kahin use karoge. Lekin bina braces ke, 
us variable ka janam us ek akele line ke baad hi turant khatam ho jata hai.Toh aisi declaration ka koi fayda nahi hota, 
isliye Java ise illegal maanta hai.

note:-koi bhi variable me default null jaroor dale Variable declare karte samay.

note:-()kya dikkat hai?
Dhyan se dekho agar identityModel null nahi hai (code if ke andar chala gaya), 
lekin SailPoint mein us ID ki Identity nahi milti (idn == null ho jata hai), toh kya hoga?
-->Java/Beanshell ka rule hai ki agar code kisi block ke andar jata hai, 
toh use har raste se kuch na kuch return milna chahiye. Agar idn null ho gaya, 
toh tumhara code bina kuch return kiye if block se bahar nikal jayega. 
SailPoint aise adhoore raste wale code par "Missing Return Statement" ka error de dega.
*/////////////
//////////*
()readOnly ka use in form and in quickLink and in Application-defination:-

1. Form Field mein (Sub-User Action rokne ke liye):-
Agar tum koi LCM Workflow ya Custom Form bana rahe ho, aur tum chahte ho ki user ko koi field dikhe toh sahi
(jaise unka First Name ya Employee ID), lekin wo ushke value/name ko change na kar sake, 
toh hum Form ke <Field> tag mein readOnly="true" lagate hain.
readOnly="true" poore field ko lock kar deta hai.Iska matlab user field ke andar ki value ko sirf READ kar sakta hai, us value ko CHANGE (edit) nahi kar sakta.

2. QuickLink / QuickLinkOptions mein (Access Control):-
Agar tum chahte ho ki kisi QuickLink (jaise Manage Identity ya View Identity)
ke andar user sirf data ko dekh sake, usme koi request submit ya edit na kar sake, 
toh wahan bhi readOnly="true" ka use hota hai.
ex QuickLink:-
<Attributes>
  <!-- Yeh bata raha hai ki kaun sa QuickLink khulne wala hai -->
  <Map>
    <entry key="quickLink" value="Manage Identity"/>
    
    <!-- 💡 YAHAN PAR JADU HAI! 
         Iski wajah se yeh poora operation 'View Only' ho jayega.
         User poori identity details dekh payega par 'Submit' button gayab ho jayega -->
    <entry key="readOnly" value="true"/>
    
    <!-- Baaki ki options jo batati hain ki kis user ka data dekhna hai -->
    <entry key="identityName" value="spadmin"/>
  </Map>
</Attributes>
ex QuickLinkOptions:-
Asli Use Case: Ek hi QuickLink ko do alag logon ke liye alag chalana
Maan lo tumhaare paas ek QuickLink hai: "View/Edit Identity". 
Tum chahte ho ki Manager apne bande ka data Edit kar sake, lekin ek normal Auditor ya HR sirf data ko Read (View) kar sake.
Toh tum QuickLink ke andar ke script/rules mein condition check karke dynamically readOnly="true" ya false set kar sakte ho:-
<?xml version='1.0' encoding='UTF-8'?>
<!DOCTYPE QuickLink PUBLIC "sailpoint.dtd" "sailpoint.dtd">
<QuickLink name="AuditorViewIdentity" 
           displayName="Auditor View Identity" 
           category="Identity Management" 
           action="viewIdentity" 
           messageKey="quicklink_auditor_view_identity">
  
  <Description>
    Yeh QuickLink sirf Auditors ke liye hai taaki wo bina kisi badlav ke Identity Cube ko read-only mode me check kar sakein.
  </Description>

  <Selector>
    <IdentitySelector>
      <MatchExpression>
        <MatchTerm name="capabilities" value="AuditAdmin"/>
      </MatchExpression>
    </IdentitySelector>
  </Selector>

  <QuickLinkOptions>
    <Attributes>
      <Map>
        <entry key="readOnly" value="true"/>
        
        <entry key="initialTab" value="attributes"/>
        
        <entry key="allowRequestForSelf" value="false"/>
        <entry key="allowRequestForOthers" value="true"/>
        
        <entry key="showApplications" value="true"/>
        <entry key="showHistory" value="true"/>
        <entry key="showRisk" value="true"/>
      </Map>
    </Attributes>
  </QuickLinkOptions>

</QuickLink>

3. Jab tum kisi Application (jaise Active Directory, JDBC, ya HR system) ke Schema configuration mein kisi attribute par 
readOnly="true" lagate ho, toh iska seedha matlab hota hai: "Yeh attribute sirf Target System se SailPoint ke andar data 
laane(Read) ke liye hai, SailPoint se wapas Target System par bhejne (Write) ke liye nahi."
ex:-
<Schema objectType="account" identityAttribute="objectGUID" displayName="Account Schema">
  <Attributes>
    
    <AttributeDefinition name="department" type="string" displayName="Department">
      <Description>User ka department jo Provisioning ke waqt update ho sakta hai</Description>
    </AttributeDefinition>

    <AttributeDefinition name="objectGUID" type="string" displayName="Object GUID" readOnly="true">
      <Description>System generated unique ID jo sirf AD se read hogi, SailPoint ise target par write nahi karega</Description>
    </AttributeDefinition>

    <AttributeDefinition name="whenCreated" type="string" displayName="Created Date" readOnly="true">
      <Description>Account kab bana tha, yeh sirf dekhne ke liye hai</Description>
    </AttributeDefinition>

  </Attributes>
</Schema>
*//////////
//////////////*
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
*////////////-------
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
()sects.setType("text"); galat hai:-Form.Section ka type "text" nahi hota. Section ka kaam sirf fields ko hold karna hota hai.
Type hamesha Field ka set kiya jata hai (jaise string, secret, boolean).

1. Duplicate Hierarchy Ki Galti (Aasan Bhasha Mein):-
SailPoint ke Form Engine ka ek strict rule hota hai: Ek pita(Parent) ke andar hi bacha(Child) baith sakta hai, 
aur ek bacha ek hi waqt par do alag-alag pitaon ka direct child nahi ho sakta.

User ne code mein kya kiya, is hierarchy (family tree) se dekhiye:-

Sahi Tarika (Standard):-
Form-> contains -> Section -> contains -> Field (fv)
(Yaani field, section ka bacha hai; aur section, form ka bacha hai).

User ki Galti:-
User ne pehle likha: sects.add(fv); (Field chala gaya Section ke andar).
Phir likha: forms.add(sects); (Section chala gaya Form ke andar).
Aur phir galti se ye line likh di: forms.add(fv);

Is aakhiri line ki wajah se SailPoint ka engine confuse ho gaya kyunki ab fv (Field) direct Form ke andar bhi baithne ki koshish 
kar raha hai aur Section ke andar bhi. Jab SailPoint iska XML convert karne jata hai, 
toh structure corrupt ho jata hai aur UI crash ho jata hai. 
Logs mein error isliye nahi aati kyunki Java ke mutabik object creation sahi hai, 
par SailPoint ka UI processor ise padh nahi paata.

()workflow kaam kya kar raha tha?
-->
### Aasan Shabdo Mein Summary (Unke Workflow Ka Asli Maqsad):-
Unka poora workflow ek **"Dynamic Survey ya FeedBack Form"** ki tarah kaam karne ke liye design kiya gaya tha. 
> **Asli Maqsad:** Jab bhi koi user QuickLink par click kare, 
toh uski screen par ek custom form pop-up ho, jisme us user ka naam pehle se likha ho (fv.setValue(launcher)),
 aur bache hue hisse mein situation ke hisab se $n$ number of naye text boxes dikhein taaki user se kuch information li ja sake. 
Lekin unka code usi **Step 3 (Form structure build karne)** ke dauran hierarchy corruption (forms.add(fv)) ki wajah se freeze ho 
gaya, isiliye workflow aage badh hi nahi paya aur form khali (load nahi hua) dikha.

1. Yeh Form aur Workflow kahan upload karein?
SailPoint IdentityIQ (IIQ) mein kisi bhi XML file (chahe woh Form ho, Workflow ho, ya Rule) 
ko upload karne ka ek hi standard tarika hota hai, jise hum "global setting ka Import" bolte hain.

()workflow ko trigger karne ka rules:-
Niyam A: Ek QuickLink Object Hona Chahiye
Aapko SailPoint mein ek QuickLink object banana padta hai jo dashboard par ek button ke roop mein dikhega. 
Us QuickLink XML ke andar aapko batana padta hai ki is button ke dabte hi kaun sa workflow chalega.

Niyam B: QuickLink Options Rule (Optional but Useful)
Agar aap chahte hain ki yeh button kis-kis employee ko dikhe (jaise sirf Managers ko dikhe, ya sirf IT team ko dikhe),
toh uske liye ek QuickLink Options Rule likha jata hai. Yeh rule sirf true ya false return karta hai yeh tay karne ke liye ki 
dashboard par button visible hoga ya nahi.

Niyam C: Identity QuickLink Id Framework (Most Important)
Aapne user ke purane code mein dekha tha ki wahan ek variable use ho raha tha: quickLinkIdentityId.
SailPoint ka yeh niyam hai ki jab aap dashboard par kisi employee ke naam ke aage jaakar custom button dabate hain, 
toh SailPoint automatic us target employee ka unique ID quickLinkIdentityId naam ke variable mein generate karke is workflow ko bhej deta hai.

Object 1: QuickLink XML (Niyam A & C ka Setup)
Yeh XML aapke SailPoint ke dashboard par ek button banayega jiska naam hoga "Dynamic Survey Portal". 
Isme action="workflow" aur workflowName="Sample Workflow" set hai, 
jo seedhe aapke custom workflow ko trigger karega aur target identity ki ID parde ke peeche pass kar dega.
->XML
<?xml version='1.0' encoding='UTF-8'?>
<!DOCTYPE QuickLink PUBLIC "sailpoint.dtd" "sailpoint.dtd">
<QuickLink action="workflow" category="SelfService" label="Dynamic Survey Portal" message="Click here to launch the dynamic questionnaire" name="Dynamic Survey Portal Link">
  <Attributes>
    <Map>
	<!-- Yeh line bata rahi hai ki button dabte hi kaunsa workflow chalana hai -->
      <entry key="workflowName" value="Sample Workflow"/>
	<!-- Isse yeh button user ke "My Services" ya dashboard par dikhne lagega -->
      <entry key="allowEveryone" value="true"/>
    </Map>
  </Attributes>
</QuickLink>

Object 2: Form XML (Sancha / Template)
Yeh aapka custom form sancha (structure) hai jo workflow ke zariye call hoga.

XML
<?xml version='1.0' encoding='UTF-8'?>
<!DOCTYPE Form PUBLIC "sailpoint.dtd" "sailpoint.dtd">
<Form name="Sample Workflow Form" type="Workflow">
  <Attributes>
    <Map>
      <entry key="pageTitle" value="Dynamic Survey Portal"/>
      <entry key="subtitle" value="Please provide the requested details below"/>
      <entry key="title" value="Information Collection Form"/>
    </Map>
  </Attributes>
  <Description>Custom template for dynamic fields placement</Description>
  <Section label="Requested Inputs" name="DynamicSection">
  <!-- Yeh khali rahega, isme runtime par fields add hongi -->
    </Section>
  <Button action="next" label="Submit Request"/>
  <Button action="back" label="Back"/>
</Form>
/////////*
1. <entry key="pageTitle" value="Dynamic Survey Portal"/>
Kahan dikhta hai: Browser ke Tab Name me (sabse upar jahan tab ka title hota hai) ya SailPoint ke main portal ki window header navigation layout me.
Kaam: Ye poorii screen ke page context ka meta title hota hai. Isse browser par name dikhta hai: Dynamic Survey Portal.

2. <entry key="title" value="Information Collection Form"/>
Kahan dikhta hai: Form panel ke sabse upar, main heading (H1) ki tarah bold me.
Kaam: Jab user browser window ke andar form ko dekhta hai, to use white ya grey box ke top par jo sabse badi heading milti hai, wo yahi hoti hai. Isse user ko pata chalta hai ki ye ek Information Collection Form hai.

3. <entry key="subtitle" value="Please provide the requested details below"/>
Kahan dikhta hai: Main heading (title) ke just niche, chote aur halke (muted) fonts me.
Kaam: Ye user ke liye ek chota sa instruction text ya help message hota hai (jaise: Please provide the requested details below), jo main title ko support karta hai taaki user ko pata chale ki aage kya karna hai.

🖥️ UI Par Layout Kaisa Dikhega?
Jab aapka Form screen par render hoga, to unka placement is tarah hoga:

+--------------------------------------------------------------+
| 🌐 Dynamic Survey Portal (<- This is pageTitle in Browser Tab)|
+--------------------------------------------------------------+
|                                                              |
|   Information Collection Form   (<- This is main 'title')     |
|   Please provide the requested details below (<- 'subtitle')  |
|   ________________________________________________________   |
|                                                              |
|   [ Requested Inputs ]                                       |
|   Target Employee:  [ amit.kumar               ]             |
|   Submitted By:     [ spadmin                  ]             |
|   Dynamic Input 1:  [__________________________]             |
|                                                              |
|   [ Submit Request ]   [ Cancel ]                            |
+--------------------------------------------------------------+-?>
*/////////

Object 3: Workflow XML (Main Engine)
Yeh poora combined workflow hai. Yeh quickLinkIdentityId ka use karke target employee ka naam nikalega, 
use form mein lock (ReadOnly) karega aur baki 'n' number of dynamic fields generate karke screen par dikhayega.

XML
<?xml version='1.0' encoding='UTF-8'?>
<!DOCTYPE Workflow PUBLIC "sailpoint.dtd" "sailpoint.dtd">
<Workflow explicitTransitions="true" name="Sample Workflow" type="IdentityLifecycle">

  <Variable input="true" name="launcher"/>
  <Variable input="true" name="quickLinkIdentityId"/>
  <Variable name="identityName"/>
  <Variable name="driveAction" output="true"/>
  <Variable name="dynamicFormObject">
    <Description>Stores the modified form object layout after script execution</Description>
  </Variable>

  <Step icon="Start" name="Start" posX="28" posY="10">
    <Transition to="Get Identity Details"/>
  </Step>

  <Step name="Get Identity Details" posX="150" posY="10" resultVariable="identityName">
    <Script>
      <Source>
        import sailpoint.object.Identity;
        
        String targetName = "Unknown";
        if (quickLinkIdentityId != null) {
            Identity idn = context.getObjectById(Identity.class, quickLinkIdentityId);
            if (idn != null) {
                targetName = idn.getName();
            }
        } else {
            targetName = launcher;
        }
        return targetName;
      </Source>
    </Script>
    <Transition to="Prepare Dynamic Form"/>
  </Step>

  <Step name="Prepare Dynamic Form" posX="300" posY="10" resultVariable="dynamicFormObject">
    <Script>
      <Source>
        import sailpoint.object.Form;
        import sailpoint.object.Form.Section;
        import sailpoint.object.Form.Field;
        
        // Template context se form layout fetch karna
        Form myForm = context.getObjectByName(Form.class, "Sample Workflow Form");
        
        if (myForm != null) {
            Form.Section baseSection = myForm.getSection("DynamicSection");
            
            if (baseSection != null) {
                // Field A: Target Employee
                Form.Field targetUserField = new Form.Field();
                targetUserField.setName("targetEmployeeName");
                targetUserField.setLabel("Target Employee");
                targetUserField.setType("string");
                targetUserField.setValue(identityName); 
                targetUserField.setReadOnly(true);
                baseSection.add(targetUserField);

                // Field B: Submitter (Launcher)
                Form.Field launcherField = new Form.Field();
                launcherField.setName("submittedBy");
                launcherField.setLabel("Submitted By");
                launcherField.setType("string");
                launcherField.setValue(launcher);
                launcherField.setReadOnly(true);
                baseSection.add(launcherField);

                // Dynamic Input Fields Loop (n=3)
                int n = 3; 
                for (int i = 1; i &lt;= n; i++) {
                    Form.Field dynamicField = new Form.Field();
                    dynamicField.setName("dynamicQuestion_" + i);
                    dynamicField.setLabel("Dynamic Input Field " + i);
                    dynamicField.setType("string");
                    dynamicField.setRequired(true);
                    baseSection.add(dynamicField);
                }
            }
        }
        return myForm; // Returns complete object graph
      </Source>
    </Script>
    <Transition to="Display Dynamic Form"/>
  </Step>

  <Step icon="Approval" name="Display Dynamic Form" posX="460" posY="10">
    <Approval owner="ref:launcher" return="driveAction">
      <Arg name="workItemType" value="Form"/>
      <Arg name="workItemForm" value="ref:dynamicFormObject"/>
    </Approval>
    <Transition to="Stop"/>
  </Step>

  <Step icon="Stop" name="Stop" posX="600" posY="10"/>

</Workflow>
//////////////*
()<Section label="Requested Inputs" name="DynamicSection">
  <!-- Yeh khali rahega, isme runtime par fields add hongi -->
    </Section> jo dynamicformobject banega wo yaha show hoga??????????
------>>>>nahi,
Iska jawab hai: dynamicFormObject is section ke andar show nahi hoga, 
balki dynamicFormObject ke ANDAR ye section khud mojud rahega.

Chalo isko aasan shabdon me samajhte hain ki jab loop chalta hai, 
to backend me sancha (Template) aur naya object kaise aaps me kaam karte hain:

1. Sample Workflow Form Kya hai? (Ek Khali Sancha)
Jo Form XML tumne banaya hai, wo ek sancha (Blueprint) hai. Us sancha me ek khali almari hai jiska naam hai DynamicSection:

XML
<Section label="Requested Inputs" name="DynamicSection">
  </Section>
2. Script Chalne Par Kya Hota Hai? (The Modification)
Step 3 (Prepare Dynamic Form) me jab tum ye line likhte ho:-
Java
Form myForm = context.getObjectByName(Form.class, "Sample Workflow Form");
To SailPoint memory me us khali sancha (Form) ki ek copy uthata hai. 
Uske baad tumhari script us sancha ke andar se us khali almari (DynamicSection) ko dhoondti hai:

Java
Form.Section baseSection = myForm.getSection("DynamicSection");
Ab, tumhara loop (for int i=1; i<=n; i++) chalta hai aur wo teen naye textboxes 
(Form.Field) banakar, is khali almari ke andar thonp (add) deta hai:
Java
baseSection.add(dynamicField); // Almari me dabba daal diya

3. dynamicFormObject Kya Banta Hai?
Jab script ke aakhri me return myForm; hota hai, to jo naya poora object banta hai, 
use humne variable diya hai dynamicFormObject.
Yani,dynamicFormObject koi field ya section nahi hai, 
balki wo us poore Form ka naya dynamic roop (Object Graph) hai, 
jiske andar DynamicSection ab khali nahi raha, 
balki usme 5 fields (Target User, Submitter, aur 3 Dynamic Inputs) bhari hui hain.

4. UI Par Kaise Show Hota Hai?
Jab Step 4 (Display Dynamic Form) chalta hai:-
XML
<Arg name="workItemForm" value="ref:dynamicFormObject"/>
To SailPoint is taiyar naye bhare hue form object (dynamicFormObject) ko uthakar browser par render kar deta hai. 
User ko screen par Requested Inputs label ke niche saari fields ek ke baad ek sequence me dikhne lagti hain.
*///////////
////////////*
()targetUserField.setValue(identityName);:-
targetUserField.setReadOnly(true); // <-- Iska connection dekho
Pehli line ne kiya: Dabbe me naam daal diya (amit.kumar).

Doosri line ne kiya: Us dabbe ko lock (freeze) kar diya taaki jo banda form bhar raha hai, 
wo us naam ko mita kar koi dusra naam na likh sake.

->💡 Is Code Ka Asli Jalwa (Fayda) Kya Hai?
Maano kal ko tumhara manager bolta hai ki "Bhai, 3 field nahi, ab hume user se 10 questions puchne hain." 
To tumko poora XML baith kar manually edit nahi karna padega. Tumhe bas is code ki sabse pehli line badalni hai:-

Java
int n = 10; // Bas ye badlo, niche ka code automatic 10 dabbe bana dega!
*/////////////
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
()dentityIQ (IIQ) mein Custom Object banane ka matlab hota hai "SailPoint ke database mein apni ek nayi table (ya data structure) banana".
SailPoint ke paas pehle se kuch standard objects hote hain jaise Identity (users ke liye), Application (target systems ke liye), 
aur Link (accounts ke liye). Lekin jab aapki company ki koi aisi requirement ho jo in standard objects mein fit nahi baithti, 
tab hum Custom Object banate hain.

-->Iska Asli Matlab Kya Hai? (Real-World Examples):-
Maan lijiye aapko SailPoint ke andar kuch aisa data store karna hai jiska users ya accounts se seedha lena-dena nahi hai, jaise:-

-->City and Branch Managers List: Aapko ek data table chahiye jisme likha ho ki "Agar city Mumbai hai, toh manager Amit hoga; agar Delhi hai, toh Rahul hoga." Yeh data aap Workflows ya Rules mein check karna chahte hain.

-->Application Risk Mapping: Ek aisi table jahan har application ke aage uski business criticality likhi ho (e.g., Active Directory = High, Zoom = Low).

-->Temporary Exclusions: Un employees ki list jinhe agle 2 mahine tak automatic certification se bahar (exclude) rakhna hai.

Yeh saara data store karne ke liye SailPoint mein pehle se koi bani-banayi jagah nahi hoti. Isi tarah ke data ko hold karne ke liye hum ek custom object banate hain, jise Custom Object bola jata hai.

Parde ke Peeche Yeh Kaise Kaam Karta Hai?
SailPoint ke database (MySQL/Oracle) mein ek table hoti hai jiska naam hai spt_custom.
Jab aap koi Custom Object banate hain, toh woh isi table ke andar ek Key-Value Pair (Attributes Map) ke roop mein jaakar save ho jata hai. Iska sabse bada fayda yeh hai ki aap pure Java Code (BeanShell) ke zariye is data ko jab chahein padh(get kar) sakte hain aur badal(update kar) sakte hain.

()Ek Simple Custom Object XML Kaisa Dikhta Hai?
-->location ka object banayenge:-

<?xml version='1.0' encoding='UTF-8'?>
<!DOCTYPE Form PUBLIC "sailpoint.dtd" "sailpoint.dtd">
<Form name="Custom Location Form" type="Workflow">
  <Attributes>
    <Map>
      <entry key="pageTitle" value="Add New Location"/>
      <entry key="title" value="Location Management Portal"/>
    </Map>
  </Attributes>
  <Section name="LocationDetails" label="Enter New Location Details">
    <Field displayName="Location Code" name="locCode" required="true" type="string">
      <Description>Example: NYC, BOM, LON</Description>
    </Field>
    <Field displayName="Location Name" name="locName" required="true" type="string">
      <Description>Example: New York, Mumbai, London</Description>
    </Field>
  </Section>
  <Button action="next" label="Save Location"/>
  <Button action="back" label="Cancel"/>
</Form>

Is workflow ke andar humne ek custom step lagaya hai—Save To Custom Object—jo user ke bhare hue inputs ko uthayega aur direct SailPoint ke Custom Object database configuration table mein naye record ke roop mein insert (commit) kar dega.

XML
<?xml version='1.0' encoding='UTF-8'?>
<!DOCTYPE Workflow PUBLIC "sailpoint.dtd" "sailpoint.dtd">
<Workflow explicitTransitions="true" name="Add Custom Location Workflow" type="Standard">

  <!-- Core variables -->
  <Variable input="true" name="launcher">
    <Description>The user executing this workflow.</Description>
  </Variable>
  <Variable name="locCode">
    <Description>Captured from form input</Description>
  </Variable>
  <Variable name="locName">
    <Description>Captured from form input</Description>
  </Variable>

  <!-- STEP 1: START -->
  <Step icon="Start" name="Start" posX="28" posY="10">
    <Transition to="Display Location Form"/>
  </Step>

  <!-- STEP 2: DISPLAY FORM (User se inputs lena) -->
  <Step icon="Approval" name="Display Location Form" posX="150" posY="10">
    <Approval owner="ref:launcher" return="locCode,locName" workItemType="Form">
      <FormRef name="Custom Location Form"/>
    </Approval>
    <Transition to="Save To Custom Object"/>
  </Step>

  <!-- STEP 3: SAVE TO CUSTOM OBJECT (Asli core logic using Custom class) -->
  <Step icon="Task" name="Save To Custom Object" posX="320" posY="10">
    <Script>
      <Source>
        import sailpoint.object.Custom;
        import sailpoint.api.SailPointContext;
        import java.util.HashMap;
        import java.util.Map;

        // 1. Database se 'Locations' naam ka custom object dhoodho
        Custom locationsObject = context.getObjectByName(Custom.class, "Locations");

        // 2. Agar object pehle se nahi bana hai, toh naya paida karo (Safety check)
        if (locationsObject == null) {
            locationsObject = new Custom();
            locationsObject.setName("Locations");
        }

        // 3. Purani locations ki list/map nikal lo
        Map currentAttributes = locationsObject.getAttributes();
        if (currentAttributes == null) {
            currentAttributes = new HashMap();
        }

        // 4. Nayi location ka Code aur Name is table map mein thonp do
        if (locCode != null &amp;&amp; locName != null) {
            currentAttributes.put(locCode.trim(), locName.trim());
            locationsObject.setAttributes(currentAttributes);

            // 5. Database mein permanently save aur lock kar do
            context.saveObject(locationsObject);
            context.commitTransaction();
            
            System.out.println("Location successfully saved: " + locCode + " -> " + locName);
        }
      </Source>
    </Script>
    <Transition to="Stop"/>
  </Step>

  <!-- STEP 4: STOP -->
  <Step icon="Stop" name="Stop" posX="480" posY="10"/>

</Workflow>
Yeh Setup Kaam Kaise Karega?
Jab koi user dashboard ke QuickLink button par click karega, toh yeh naya workflow chalega.
Sabse pehle unke samne ek neat aur clean popup box (Custom Location Form) khulega jisme do empty text box honge.
Maan lijiye user ne bhara: Code = DEL, Name = Delhi.
Jaise hi user "Save Location" dabaayega, workflow turant Save To Custom Object step par aayega aur 
SailPoint database ke spt_custom table ke andar "Locations" namak record mein jaakar DEL=Delhi ko permanently chipka dega.
Database mein Locations naam ka row/record "Workflow ke andar likhi BeanShell Script" banati hai, Form nahi.

///////////*
()<Approval owner="ref:launcher" return="locCode,locName" workItemType="Form">
      <FormRef name="Custom Location Form"/>
</Approval>:-
-->Short me:-return="locCode,locName":-
Yeh system ko bata raha hai ki "Form submit hone par mujhe poora kachra nahi chahiye, 
bas Location Code aur Location Name nikal kar de do."

-->Agar aap return specify nahi karenge, toh system poora ka poora form ka data utha kar agle step ko bhej dega.
Udaharan ke liye, jab user form bharta hai toh usme yeh sab hota hai:-
1. Form ki Technical Fields:-
formId / transactionId: Har form ka ek lamba sa unique number hota hai (jaise: FRM-98342-XJZ).
submissionDate / timestamp: Form kis date aur exact second par submit hua.
ipAddress: User kis computer ya network se form bhar raha tha.
browserType: Chrome use kiya, Safari, ya Edge.

2. User ki Personal/Basic Details:-
createdBy / launcherEmail: Form bharne wale ka email id ya employee code.
launcherDepartment: Launcher ka department (jaise: HR, IT, Finance).
launcherManager: Uske manager ka naam.

3. Form ke andar ki Doosri Fields:-
Maan lijiye location form me user se aur bhi baatein poochhi gayi thin:
estimatedStaff: Us naye office me kitne log baithenge.
officeType: Office rented (kiraye par) hai ya owned (khud ka).
remarks / comments: User ne form bharte waqt agar koi extra note likha ho.

4. Next, Cancel ya Submit Buttons (UI Buttons):-
Jab user form par Submit ya Cancel button dabata hai, toh system ke liye yeh sirf ek temporary 'Event' (action) hota hai.
Agar aap return="locCode,locName" specify nahi karenge, toh system aage yeh data bhi bhej sakta hai ki: clickedButton="Submit" ya actionPerformed="Next".

5. Dynamic Fields (Badalne wali fields):-
Dynamic fields woh hoti hain jo user ke selection ke mutabiq achanak form par dikhne lagti hain.
Example: Maan lijiye form me ek dropdown tha: "Country". User ne select kiya "India". 
Ab dynamic field khul gayi: "State" aur "City".
Agar user ne 4-5 dynamic fields bhari hain (jaise State, City, Pin Code, Address Line 1), ko bhi bhej deta hai.
*///////////
---------------------------------------------------------------------->>>>>>>>>---------------------------------------------
1. Plan-Level vs AttributeRequest Level (Sancha):-
SailPoint mein jab koi access request aati hai, toh ek ProvisioningPlan banta hai.
Plan-Level (Main Header): Yeh form ka sabse upar ka hissa hai (Bada Dabba).
AttributeRequest Level (Line Items): Yeh form ke andar ki tables ya lines hain jahan likha hota hai ki 
kaunsa group ya role chahiye (Chote Dabbe).

2. Overwrite Ki Asli Bimari (Problem):-
Maan lijiye ek manager ne ek hi baar mein ek employee ke liye do alag-alag access maange:
Active Directory Group: Yeh sirf 10 din ke liye chahiye (Temporary).
SAP Application Role: Yeh hamesha ke liye chahiye (Permanent).
Jab SailPoint ka LCM Workflow in dono requests ko process karne ke liye ek bada plan banata hai aur unhe Merge (Aapas mein jodna) karta hai, toh engine ek bada ghumav leta hai.
Woh individual items ki alag-alag dates ko dhyan mein rakhne ke bajay, poore plan ke Header (Plan-Level) par jo main date range likhi hoti hai, use uthakar sab par thonp (overwrite) deta hai.
Iska nateeja yeh hota hai ki jo access aapne temporary maanga tha, uski date mitt(clean) ho jati hai aur dono access permanent ya phir galat dates ke sath process ho jate hain.

3. Sunrise aur Sunset Ka Sahi Ilaaj (Solution):-
SailPoint mein temporary access ko handle karne ke liye do attributes hote hain:-
sysSunrise (Start Date): Is din access automatic active hoga.
sysSunset (End Date): Is din access automatic chhin (deprovision) jayega.
Statement kehta hai ki agar aapko is overwrite se bachna hai, toh in dono dates ko poore plan par mat lagao. 
Inhe seedhe AttributeRequest (yaani specific group ya role ke dabbe) ke andar daal do.

<?xml version='1.0' encoding='UTF-8'?>
<!DOCTYPE Workflow PUBLIC "sailpoint.dtd" "sailpoint.dtd">
<Workflow explicitTransitions="true" name="Custom Safe Provisioning Workflow" type="Standard">

  <Variable input="true" name="identityName">
    <Description>The target user who needs access (e.g., Shiva).</Description>
  </Variable>
  <Variable input="true" name="application">
    <Description>The name of the target application (e.g., Oracle ERP or AD).</Description>
  </Variable>
  <Variable input="true" name="requestedItemsList">
    <Description>List of Maps containing responsibilityValue, startDateVal, and endDateVal.</Description>
  </Variable>

  <Step icon="Start" name="Start" posX="28" posY="10">
    <Transition to="Custom Provisioning Engine"/>
  </Step>

  <Step icon="Task" name="Custom Provisioning Engine" posX="180" posY="10">
    <Script>
      <Source>
        <![CDATA[                                              //  yaha cdata ke rang ko hatane ke liye]]>
        import sailpoint.object.ProvisioningPlan;
        import sailpoint.object.ProvisioningPlan.AccountRequest;
        import sailpoint.object.ProvisioningPlan.AttributeRequest;
        import sailpoint.object.ProvisioningProject;
        import sailpoint.api.Provisioner;
        import java.text.SimpleDateFormat;
        import java.util.Date;
        import java.util.List;
        import java.util.Map;

        // Date format initialize karein
        SimpleDateFormat df = new SimpleDateFormat("yyyy-MM-dd"); 
        boolean hasErrors = false;

        // Plan aur AccountRequest ka creation loop se bahar
        ProvisioningPlan provisioningPlan = new ProvisioningPlan();
        provisioningPlan.setIdentity(context.getObjectByName(sailpoint.object.Identity.class, identityName));

        AccountRequest acctReq = new AccountRequest(
            ProvisioningPlan.AccountRequest.Operation.Modify,
            application, 
            null, 
            identityName
        );

        // Safety check taaki list khali hone par crash na ho
        if (requestedItemsList != null && !requestedItemsList.isEmpty()) {
            
            // Loop ke andar har item ko securely process karenge
            for (Object itemObj : requestedItemsList) {
                Map item = (Map) itemObj;
                
                String responsibilityValue = (String) item.get("responsibilityValue");
                String startDateVal = (String) item.get("startDateVal");
                String endDateVal = (String) item.get("endDateVal");

                if (responsibilityValue != null) {
                    try {
                        // Naya AttributeRequest banana loop ke andar
                        AttributeRequest attrReq = new AttributeRequest(
                            "entitlements",
                            ProvisioningPlan.Operation.Add,
                            responsibilityValue
                        );

                        // Sunrise logic - TRY block ke andar taaki parsing error trap ho sake
                        if (startDateVal != null && startDateVal.trim().length() > 0) {
                            Date sDate = df.parse(startDateVal.trim());
                            attrReq.setAddDate(sDate);          // Native API
                            attrReq.setAttribute("sunrise", sDate); // Metadata Tagging
                        }

                        // Sunset logic
                        if (endDateVal != null && endDateVal.trim().length() > 0) {
                            Date eDate = df.parse(endDateVal.trim());
                            attrReq.setRemoveDate(eDate);       // Native API
                            attrReq.setAttribute("sunset", eDate);  // Metadata Tagging
                        }

                        // Agar upar sab sahi raha, toh hi request jama hogi
                        acctReq.add(attrReq);

                    } catch (Exception e) {
                        // Agar date parsing fail hui, toh hasErrors true hoga aur loop aage badhega
                        hasErrors = true;
                        System.out.println("Error parsing dates for item [" + responsibilityValue + "] of user " + identityName + ": " + e.getMessage());
                    }
                }
            }
        }

        // AccountRequest ko Plan mein joda
        provisioningPlan.add(acctReq);

        // SAFETY CHECK: Agar poore loop mein kahin bhi error aayi, toh execute nahi hoga
        if (!hasErrors) {
            Provisioner provisioner = new Provisioner(context);
            ProvisioningProject proj = provisioner.compile(provisioningPlan);
            provisioner.execute(proj);
            
            System.out.println("Custom Provisioning Executed Successfully for: " + identityName);
        } else {
            System.out.println("Execution Aborted! One or more items had date parsing issues for user: " + identityName);
        }
        ]]>
      </Source>
    </Script>
    <Transition to="Stop"/>
  </Step>

  <Step icon="Stop" name="Stop" posX="350" posY="10"/>

</Workflow>
////////////////*
()variables ko value koun de raha hai???????????????????????
()variables me value koun dega?
-<Variable input="true" name="identityName">
<Variable input="true" name="application">
<Variable input="true" name="requestedItemsList">

-->dekho ki ishke variables me value koun de raha hai:-
1. LCM Provisioning / Request Access UI se (Most Common):-
Agar yeh workflow Kisi Access Request page (Manage User Access) se trigger ho raha hai, 
toh jab end-user ya manager UI par jaakar koi role ya entitlement select karta hai, 
toh SailPoint ka core engine internally in variables ko populate karta hai:-

--identityName: Jis target user (jaise Shiva) ke liye access request kiya gaya hai, uski Identity ka naam.

--application: Jis application (jaise Oracle ERP ya AD) ka entitlement select kiya gaya hai.

--requestedItemsList: Jo roles/entitlements, unki custom start date (Sunrise) aur end date (Sunset) select ki gayi hain, 
unka poora data ek List of Maps ke roop mein pass hota hai.

2. Kisi Parent Workflow ke <Step> Call se:-
Agar is workflow ko kisi dusre bade workflow (jaise LCM Provisioning ya koi Custom Master Workflow) 
ke andar se ek sub-process ya child workflow ki tarah call kiya ja raha hai, 
toh parent workflow ka step isko value de raha hoga.

Uss parent workflow mein code kuch aisa dikhega:-
XML
<Step name="Call Custom Safe Provisioning" subWorkflow="Custom Safe Provisioning Workflow">
  <Arg name="identityName" value="ref:identityName"/>
  <Arg name="application" value="ref:applicationName"/>
  <Arg name="requestedItemsList" value="ref:cartItems"/> </Step>
  
3. "Run Rule" Task ya BeanShell Script se (Testing/Automation)
Agar is workflow ko manually test karne ke liye kisi background task ya Custom Rule se run kiya ja raha hai, toh developer ne code ke zariye map bana kar isme values pass ki hongi.
Example background launcher code:-//Complete Workflower Launch Script:-
import sailpoint.object.Identity;
import sailpoint.object.Workflow;
import sailpoint.api.Workflower;
import java.util.HashMap;
import java.util.Map;
import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.List;
import org.apache.commons.logging.Log;
import org.apache.commons.logging.LogFactory;

// Logging initialize karein (SailPoint debugging ke liye sabse best hai)
Log log = LogFactory.getLog("custom.rule.workflowLauncher");

try {
    // 1. Launch Arguments Map taiyar karein
    Map launchArgs = new HashMap();
    
    // Core variables pass karein
    launchArgs.put("identityName", "Shiva");
    launchArgs.put("application", "Oracle ERP");

    // 2. requestedItemsList (List of Maps) taiyar karein
    List itemsList = new ArrayList();
    
    // Pehla Item/Responsibility
    Map item1 = new HashMap();
    item1.put("responsibilityValue", "Finance_Manager");
    item1.put("startDateVal", "2026-06-01");
    item1.put("endDateVal", "2026-12-31");
    itemsList.add(item1);
    
    // Agar aapko ek se zyada items bhejne hain, toh aap isi tarah add kar sakte hain:
    /*
    Map item2 = new HashMap();
    item2.put("responsibilityValue", "General_Ledger_Viewer");
    item2.put("startDateVal", "2026-07-15");
    item2.put("endDateVal", "2026-08-15");
    itemsList.add(item2);
    */

    // List ko final launch arguments mein daalein
    launchArgs.put("requestedItemsList", itemsList);

    // 3. Workflow ka naam define karein jo aapko launch karna hai
    String workflowName = "Custom Safe Provisioning Workflow";
    
    // 4. Workflower class ka object banayein aur workflow launch karein
    Workflower workflower = new Workflower(context);
    
    // Parameters: launch(workflowName, caseName, launcher, arguments)
    // caseName null rakhne par SailPoint automatic unique name generate kar leta hai
    workflower.launch(workflowName, null, null, launchArgs);
    
    log.info("Workflow '" + workflowName + "' successfully launched for identity: Shiva");
    return "Workflow Launched Successfully!";

} catch (Exception e) {
    log.error("Error while launching workflow: " + e.getMessage(), e);
    return "Error: " + e.getMessage();
}
//////////*
()workflower.launch(workflowName, caseName, launcher, launchArgs);:-
Parameter             Aapke Code Mein Value                                      Iska Asli Matlab Kya Hai?
workflowName------"Custom Safe Provisioning Workflow"-------------------Kaun sa workflow chalana hai? Yeh engine ko batata hai ki kis unique Workflow definition ko uthana hai.
caseName---------------------null---------------------------------------Workflow instance ka naam kya hoga? Agar aap yahan null dete hain, toh SailPoint khud se ek unique naam generate kar leta hai (jaise: Custom Safe Provisioning Workflow - 15). Agar aap chahein toh yahan apna custom naam jaise "Shiva - Oracle ERP Provisioning" bhi de sakte hain.
launcher---------------------null---------------------------------------Is workflow ko start karne wala kaun hai? Agar aap null chhodte hain, toh jo current logged-in user ya system background process ise run kar rahi hai, use hi launcher maan liya jata hai. Aap chahein toh yahan kisi specific Identity object ka naam de sakte hain.
launchArgs---------------launchArgs (Map)-------------------------------Workflow ke andar kya data bhejna hai? Yeh sabse zaroori hissa hai. Humne jo Map banaya tha jisme identityName, application, aur requestedItemsList daala tha, woh isi ke zariye workflow ke <Variable> blocks mein transfer hota hai.
*/////////
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
()1. responsibilityValue Kya Hai?
responsibilityValue asal mein ek Key (naam):-
Iska asan matlab hai Target Attribute ki Value—yaani jo Role,Responsibility,ya Group aap target user(jaise Shiva) ko dena chahte hain.
Agar aap Oracle ERP mein access de rahe hain, toh yeh kisi Responsibility ka naam hoga (jaise "Finance_Manager" ya "GL_User").
Agar aap Active Directory (AD) mein access de rahe hain, toh yeh kisi AD Group ka naam hoga (jaise "CN=Finance-Dept,OU=Groups,DC=domain,DC=com").

()item.get("responsibilityValue");:-
->Map item1 = new HashMap();
item1.put("responsibilityValue", "Finance_Manager");
item1.put("startDateVal", "2026-06-01");
->toh "Finance_Manager" return kaega.

()attrReq.setAddDate(sDate);  kya karta hai?        // Native API for sunrise timing
attrReq.setAttribute("sunrise", sDate); // Explicit metadata tagging
()attrReq.setRemoveDate(eDate);    kya karta hai?   // Native API for sunset timing
attrReq.setAttribute("sunset", eDate); kya karta hai? // Explicit metadata tagging

-->1. Sunrise Logic (Access kab chalu hoga?)
-->attrReq.setAddDate(sDate);
Kya karta hai? Yeh SailPoint ka Native (In-built) System Method hai. Yeh seedhe backend engine ko order deta hai ki is access ko abhi active mat karo, balki database mein ek schedule banakar chhod do.
Asli Kaam: Jo date aapne sDate mein di hai, us din SailPoint ka background task automatic chalega aur user (jaise Shiva) ko access de dega.

-->attrReq.setAttribute("sunrise", sDate);
Kya karta hai? Yeh request ke upar ek Custom Tag (Chit/Label) chipka deta hai.
Asli Kaam: Bahut baar provisioning ke dauran native date aage pass nahi ho paati. Yeh tag backup ka kaam karta hai. Agar aapko aage jaakar kisi rule ya workflow mein check karna ho ki "is role ki start date kya thi?", toh aap is tag se value nikal sakte hain.

2. Sunset Logic (Access kab khatam hoga?)
-->attrReq.setRemoveDate(eDate);
Kya karta hai? Yeh SailPoint ka Native System Method hai End Date set karne ke liye.
Asli Kaam: Yeh backend engine ko officially bata deta hai ki eDate aate hi is user se yeh role automatic wapas chheen (deprovision) lena hai. 
Iske liye kisi insan ko manually access hatane ki zaroorat nahi padti.core engine deprovision ka plan generate karke execute kar deta hai.

-->attrReq.setAttribute("sunset", eDate);
Kya karta hai? Thik sunrise ki tarah, yeh bhi ek Custom Tag (Chit/Label) hai jo end date ke liye lagaya jata hai.
Asli Kaam: Yeh auditing aur tracking ke liye kaam aata hai. Jab aap access request ki history ya approval screens dekhenge, toh wahan yeh tag saaf dikhayega ki access kab expire hone wala hai.
*///////////
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
()Asli Requirement Kya Hai? (Company Phone Reminder)
User ne ek aisa custom workflow banaya hai jo continuously users ke Identity Attributes 
(jaise unka department, title wagera) ko check karta rehta hai.
Jaise hi kisi employee ka data badalta hai, workflow parde ke peeche yeh filters lagata hai:-
Kya us bande ka Role Code badla hai?
Ya 
kya uska Lifecycle State (jaise Active se Leaver, ya Contractor se Full-Time) badla hai?
Aur sath hi, kya us user ke paas "Company Phone" ka ek specific access profile pehle se hai?
Maqsad: Agar unka role ya state badla hai aur unke paas company phone hai, 
toh yeh workflow HR/Admin team ko ek Email Alert bhejega. Yeh alert ek reminder ki tarah kaam karega ki "Bhai, 
is bande ka status badal gaya hai, check karo ki ise abhi bhi company phone ki zaroorat hai ya nahi!"

()template email:-
<?xml version='1.0' encoding='UTF-8'?>
<!DOCTYPE EmailTemplate PUBLIC "sailpoint.dtd" "sailpoint.dtd">
<EmailTemplate name="Cellphone Certification Notification" subject="Cellphone Certification Required">
  <Body>
    A change to the following user's Lifecycle State or Primary Role Code has been detected.
    The user's cell phone possession should now be reviewed and certified.

    Name: $displayName
    Employee ID: $employeeId

    Regards,
    IdentityIQ Governance Team
  </Body>
</EmailTemplate>

///////////////*
()subject kya hai?
-->Is email template mein subject yeh hai:-
"Cellphone Certification Required"
Iska simple matlab:-
Jab aap kisi ko email bhejte hain, toh jo heading inbox mein dikhai deti hai, use subject kehte hain.
Yahan subject="Cellphone Certification Required" ka matlab hai ki jab yeh email kisi ke paas jayega, 
toh use subject line mein "Cellphone Certification Required" (yani Mobile Ka Certification Zaroori Hai) likha hua dikhega.

*//////////////

<?xml version='1.0' encoding='UTF-8'?>
<!DOCTYPE Workflow PUBLIC "sailpoint.dtd" "sailpoint.dtd">
<Workflow explicitTransitions="true" name="Cellphone Certification Reminder Workflow" type="IdentityLifecycle">

  <!-- 1. Input Variables jo Provisioning/Lifecycle Event se aayenge -->
  <Variable input="true" name="identityName">
    <Description>The name (username) of the identity that changed.</Description>
  </Variable>
  <Variable name="displayName">
    <Description>Display name for email context.</Description>
  </Variable>
  <Variable name="employeeId">
    <Description>Employee ID for email context.</Description>
  </Variable>

  <!-- STEP 1: START -->
  <Step icon="Start" name="Start" posX="28" posY="10">
    <Transition to="Check Role and Phone Access"/>
  </Step>

  <!-- STEP 2: LOOP AND CHECK LOGIC (Pure IIQ Context Script) -->
  <Step icon="Task" name="Check Role and Phone Access" posX="150" posY="10">
    <Script>
      <Source>
        import sailpoint.object.Identity;
        import sailpoint.object.Bundle;
        import java.util.List;

        boolean sendEmail = false;

        if (identityName != null) {
            // 1. Context use karke database se target user ka object nikala
            Identity identity = context.getObjectByName(Identity.class, identityName);
            
            if (identity != null) {
                // Email variables populate kar lo taaki bad mein khali na jayein
                workflow.put("displayName", identity.getDisplayName());
                workflow.put("employeeId", identity.getStringAttribute("identificationNumber")); // ya jo bhi tumhara custom attribute ID ho

                // 2. Loop Through Access Items: User ke saare Assigned Roles/Access Profiles par loop chalao
                List assignedRoles = identity.getAssignedRoles();
                if (assignedRoles != null) {
                    for (Bundle role : assignedRoles) {
                        // User ki purani galti yahan fix hui - Item name check loop ke andar safely
                        if ("Cellphone Owner".equals(role.getName())) {
                            sendEmail = true;
                            break; // Target access mil gaya, loop se bahar nikal jao
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        
        // Workflow ko batao ki aage mail bhejni hai ya nahi
        workflow.put("isCellphoneOwner", sendEmail);
      </Source>
    </Script>
    <!-- Agar condition true hui toh Send Email step par jao, nahi toh direct Stop -->
    <Transition to="Send Certification Email" condition="script:workflow.get(&quot;isCellphoneOwner&quot;) == true"/>
    <Transition to="Stop"/>
  </Step>

  <!-- STEP 3: SEND EMAIL STEP (Using Standard IIQ Email Engine) -->
  <Step icon="Message" name="Send Certification Email" posX="320" posY="10">
    <Script>
      <Source>
        import sailpoint.object.EmailOptions;
        import sailpoint.object.EmailTemplate;
        import java.util.HashMap;
        import java.util.Map;

        // 1. Email Context Map taiyar karo (Variables mapping)
        Map emailArgs = new HashMap();
        emailArgs.put("displayName", displayName);
        emailArgs.put("employeeId", employeeId);

        // 2. IIQ options set karo
        EmailOptions options = new EmailOptions();
        options.setVariables(emailArgs);
        options.setTo("Bilbo.Baggins@theshire.com");

        // 3. System se email template uthao aur fire kar do
        // Note: Aap 'Cellphone Certification Notification' naam ka EmailTemplate IIQ me bana sakte hain
        context.sendEmailNotification(context.getObjectByName(EmailTemplate.class, "Cellphone Certification Notification"), options);
        
        System.out.println("Certification Email sent successfully for user: " + displayName);
      </Source>
    </Script>
    <Transition to="Stop"/>
  </Step>

  <!-- STEP 4: STOP -->
  <Step icon="Stop" name="Stop" posX="480" posY="10"/>

</Workflow>
/////////////*
()workflow.put("isCellphoneOwner", sendEmail); kya karta hai?
-->workflow.put("isCellphoneOwner", sendEmail); line ka seedha matlab hai:-
"Aapke code ke andar jo faisla (sendEmail = true ya false) hua hai, 
use workflow ke dabba (memory) mein ek pakka tag lagakar save kar dena,
taaki code ke khatam hone ke baad bhi workflow us faisle ko yaad rakh sake."

()1. workflow.put() Kya Kaam Karta Hai? (The Courier Boy)
BeanShell script ke andar jo sendEmail variable hai, woh sirf us chote se <Script> block ke andar hi zinda rehta hai. 
Use SailPoint ke pure workflow ka dimaag nahi pehchanta.
workflow.put("Key", Value) karne se SailPoint is data ko pure workflow ke context mein global bana deta hai.
Ab "isCellphoneOwner" naam ka ek naya temporary variable workflow case ke andar register ho jata hai, 
jiske paas true ya false ka data hota hai.
()SailPoint IdentityIQ ke andar workflow.put("key", value); ek tarah ka "Memory Storage Command" hai.
Aasan bhasha mein kahein toh: "Yeh aapke local BeanShell script ke andar chal rahe kisi variable ke data ko uthakar, 
pooray Workflow ke global memory dabba (Context) mein hamesha ke liye daal deta hai."

()context.sendEmailNotification(context.getObjectByName(EmailTemplate.class, "Cellphone Certification Notification"), options);
-->context.sendEmailNotification( EmailTemplate, EmailOptions );
Agar asan shabdo mein kahein: "Yeh SailPoint ke Email Engine ko order deti hai ki database se 
'Cellphone Certification Notification' naam ka template uthao, usme 'options' ke andar ka data bharo, 
aur mail turant deliver kar do."

-->1. Pehla Part: context.getObjectByName(EmailTemplate.class, "Cellphone Certification Notification"):-
Yeh kya karta hai? Yeh SailPoint ke database mein jaakar us Email Template object ko dhoodhta aur load karta hai jiska naam 
"Cellphone Certification Notification" hai.

-->2. Doosra Part: options:-
Yeh kya karta hai? Yeh EmailOptions ka object hai jise aapne theek is line ke upar wale code mein taiyar kiya tha. 
Iske paas do sabse zaroori cheezein hoti hain:
To Address (options.setTo(...)): Mail kisko bhejni hai (jaise aapke code mein "Bilbo.Baggins@theshire.com" set hai).
Variables Mapping (options.setVariables(...)):Template ke andar jo $displayName aur $employeeId ke khali dabbe(placeholders) the,
unme asli values (jaise Shiva aur EMP123) ko fit karne ka data is options ke paas hota hai.
*/////////////

()Haan bhai, SailPoint IdentityIQ (IIQ) mein is poore setup ko automatic chalane ke liye aur filters check karne ke liye ek 
bahut zaroori Rule lagta hai, jise hum IdentityTrigger Rule bolte hain.
1. IdentityTrigger Rule (Sabse Zaroori Rule)
Jab kisi user ka profile badalta hai, toh yeh Rule check karta hai ki kya sach mein uska Role Code ya Lifecycle State badla hai?
Agar badla hota hai, toh yeh rule true return karta hai, jisse aapka workflow apne aap chal jata hai.

Aap is Trigger Rule XML ko SailPoint mein import kar sakte hain:

<?xml version='1.0' encoding='UTF-8'?>
<!DOCTYPE Rule PUBLIC "sailpoint.dtd" "sailpoint.dtd">
<Rule name="Cellphone Trigger Attribute Change Rule" type="IdentityTrigger">
  <Description>Yeh rule check karta hai ki user ka Role Code ya Lifecycle State badla hai ya nahi.</Description>
  <Source>
    <![CDATA[                                       //]]> bash color change 
    import sailpoint.object.Identity;

    boolean triggerWorkflow = false;

    // FIX: 'oldIdentity' ko badal kar 'previousIdentity' kar diya gaya hai, kyunki SailPoint ka system yahi naam pehchanta hai
    if (newIdentity != null && previousIdentity != null) {
        
        // 1. Check karo kya Lifecycle State badla hai?
        String oldState = previousIdentity.getLifecycleState();
        String newState = newIdentity.getLifecycleState();
        
        // 2. Check karo kya Role Code badla hai?
        String oldRole = (String) previousIdentity.getAttribute("roleCode");
        String newRole = (String) newIdentity.getAttribute("roleCode");

        // Agar dono mein se kuch bhi badla (change) hua hai, toh trigger ko true kar do
        if ((newState != null && !newState.equals(oldState)) || (newRole != null && !newRole.equals(oldRole))) {
            triggerWorkflow = true;
        }
    }

    return triggerWorkflow; // Agar true return hua, toh workflow trigger ho jayega
    ]]>
  </Source>
</Rule>
//////////*
1. previousIdentity.getLifecycleState(); Kya Return Karega?
(Note: Jaise humne baat ki, oldIdentity ki jagah SailPoint mein previousIdentity hota hai)
Kya return karega: Yeh user ka badlav hone se theek pehle ka (purana) Lifecycle State return karega.
Example: Maan lijiye Shiva abhi tak company mein kaam kar rahe the, toh unka purana state database mein "active" tha. 
Yeh line wahan se "active" return karegi.

()2. newIdentity.getLifecycleState(); Kya Return Karega?
Kya return karega: Yeh user ka naya (updated) Lifecycle State return karega jo HR system se badal kar abhi-abhi SailPoint ke paas aaya hai, 
lekin abhi tak database mein completely save nahi hua hai.
Example: Maan lijiye Shiva ne company se resign kar diya aur HR system mein unka status "Terminated" ho gaya. 
Jab SailPoint use aggregate karega, toh yeh line naya status "terminated" return karegi.

()(String) previousIdentity.getAttribute("roleCode");:-
Kya return karega: User ke role change hone se theek pehle ka (purana) Role Code.
Example: Maan lijiye Shiva pehle ek Developer the, toh unka purana role code database mein "DEV_01" tha. Yeh line wahan se "DEV_01" return karegi.

()(String) newIdentity.getAttribute("roleCode");:-
Kya return karega: HR aggregation ya identity refresh ke baad jo user ka naya (updated) Role Code aaya hai, yeh use return karega.
Example: Shiva ka promotion ho gaya aur woh Manager ban gaye. Naya data aaya "MGR_05". Yeh line wahan se "MGR_05" return karegi.

1. Ek Simple Example Se Samjhein:-
Maan lijiye aapki company mein alag-alag departments hain. 
Agar SailPoint mein pure-pure designation ke naam (jaise "Senior Software Engineer Lead") save karenge, 
toh code likhne mein aur databases match karne mein dikkat aati hai. Isiliye unhe ek short code de diya jata hai:-

Employee Designation (Pura Naam)	roleCode (Short Code)
Java Web Developer-----------------------"DEV_01"
Finance Manager--------------------------"FIN_MGR"
HR Administrator-------------------------"HR_ADMIN"
Database Architect-----------------------"DBA_SR"
*///////////

()2. Lifecyle Event Configuration (Niyam):-
Upar wale Rule aur Workflow ko aapas mein jodne ke liye SailPoint mein ek Lifecycle Event banana padta hai. 
Isme hum batate hain ki jab bhi koi Identity Modify (badal) ho, toh upar wala Trigger Rule chalao, aur agar rule true bole, 
toh humara main Workflow shuru kar do.

<?xml version='1.0' encoding='UTF-8'?>
<!DOCTYPE Configuration PUBLIC "sailpoint.dtd" "sailpoint.dtd">
<Configuration name="CompanyPhoneEventConfig">
  <Attributes>
    <Map>
      <!-- Yeh script parde ke peeche chalegi aur aapke naye event ko purani list mein jod degi -->
      <entry key="lifecycleEvents">
        <value>
          <List>
            <IdentityLifecycleEvent name="Company Phone Certification Event" type="Alert" lostAccess="false">
              
              <!-- 1. Kaunsa workflow chalana hai -->
              <WorkflowRef name="Cellphone Certification Reminder Workflow"/>
              
              <!-- 2. Kaunsa trigger rule check karna hai -->
              <TriggerRuleRef name="Cellphone Trigger Attribute Change Rule"/>
              
            </IdentityLifecycleEvent>
          </List>
        </value>
      </entry>
    </Map>
  </Attributes>
</Configuration>
//////////////////*
()<entry key="lifecycleEvents"> ka matlab:-
SailPoint ke andar jitne bhi Identity lifecycle events hote hain (jaise Joiner, Mover, Leaver), 
yeh unhi ki list mein ek naya custom event jod raha hai.

()<IdentityLifecycleEvent name="Company Phone Certification Event" type="Alert" lostAccess="false">
name: Is event ka naam rakh diya gaya hai "Company Phone Certification Event".
type="Alert": Iska matlab yeh event tab trigger hoga jab SailPoint ke andar koi alert ya attribute badlega (jaise manager badalna, status active hona, ya phone status change hona).

()<WorkflowRef name="Cellphone Certification Reminder Workflow"/>:-
Jaise hi yeh event sach hoga (trigger hoga), yeh turant backend mein Cellphone Certification Reminder Workflow naam ke workflow ko chalu (launch) kar dega.

()The Decision: * Agar Rule ne return true; kiya: Toh SailPoint samajh jata hai ki condition match ho gayi hai. 
Woh turant iske upar waale tag <WorkflowRef name="Cellphone Certification Reminder Workflow"/> ko active karke workflow chalu kar deta hai.

Real-World Example Se Samjhein (Ye Kaise Kaam Karega?):-
Maan lijiye Shiva ko company se ek naya Cellphone milta hai aur HR system ya Active Directory mein unka phone attribute update hota hai:
Attribute Change: SailPoint mein identity refresh task chalta hai aur dekhta hai ki Shiva ka phone data badal gaya hai.
Rule Validation: Yeh Cellphone Trigger Attribute Change Rule turant check karta hai aur bolta hai—"Haan, Shiva ka phone status badla hai, event trigger karo!"
Event Fire: Company Phone Certification Event active ho jata hai.
Workflow Launch: Parde ke peeche Cellphone Certification Reminder Workflow launch ho jata hai, jo Shiva ke paas ek policy certification ya reminder bhej deta hai ki "Aapko phone mil gaya hai, iski policy sign karein."

*//////////////////
//////////////////*
()rule ko kishi run rule task me dalna hai:-for run rule:-nahi kyuki:-

<TriggerRuleRef name="Cellphone Trigger Attribute Change Rule"/>
<WorkflowRef name="Cellphone Certification Reminder Workflow"/>
Iska matlab yeh hai ki yeh dono cheezein ab ek Auto-Pilot Engine ban chuki hain. 
Inhe alag se kisi task mein daal kar chalane ki zaroorat nahi hoti.

()Toh Phir Yeh Rule Chalu Kaise Hoga? (Asli Flow)
Aapko bas SailPoint ke standard task "Identity Refresh" ko chalana hai. Parde ke peeche ka flow aisa hoga:
Aap Identity Refresh Task chalayenge (Jo har company mein pehle se bana hota hai aur daily chalta hai).
Us Identity Refresh Task ke andar ek checkbox hota hai: "Check Identity Trigger Events". Aapko bas us checkbox ko True (Checked) rakhna hai.
Jaise hi Refresh Task chalega, woh har ek user ke profile ko scan karega.
Scan karte waqt, SailPoint aapke is Trigger Rule ko automatic parde ke peeche bulaega aur puchega—"Bhai check kar, kya is user ka Role ya Lifecycle State badla hai?"
Agar badla hoga, toh aapka rule kahega true, aur SailPoint automatic aapke Workflow ko wahin se trigger kar dega.

()Yeh problem SailPoint IdentityIQ (IIQ) ke workflows mein tab aati hai jab hum dynamic forms par kaam karte hain. 
User keh raha hai ki unka workflow baaki sab kuch sahi kar raha hai—form screen par aa raha hai, 
dropdown ya textboxes (display-types) bhi sahi dikh rahe hain—lekin jo fields woh dynamic tarike se badhana (extending) chahte hain, 
woh screen par gayab hain (nahi aa rahi hain).

          import sailpoint.object.EmailTemplate; 
          if(!"new".equals(templateId)) {
            EmailTemplate t=context.getObjectById(EmailTemplate.class, templateId);
            if(t!=null) {
              workflow.put("templateName", t.getName());
            }
          }

                  import sailpoint.object.EmailTemplate;
                  import sailpoint.object.QueryOptions;
                  import java.util.ArrayList;
                  import java.util.Iterator;
                  import java.util.List;
                       
                  List items=new ArrayList();
                  ArrayList item=new ArrayList();
                  item.add("new");
                  item.add("-- Create new email template --");
                  items.add(item);
                                    
                  QueryOptions qo = new QueryOptions(); 
                  qo.setOrderBy("name");           

                  Iterator it = context.search(EmailTemplate.class, qo, "name,id");                   
                  while ( (null != it) &amp;&amp; (it.hasNext()) ) {
                     Object [] thisTemplate = it.next();
                     String templateName = thisTemplate[0];
                     String templateId = thisTemplate[1];
                     item=new ArrayList();
                     item.add(templateId);
                     item.add(templateName);
                     items.add(item);
                  }
                  return items;
                </Source>

flow Select Email Template step ka:-
Form Load Hona: Jaise hi workflow is step par aayega, <AllowedValuesDefinition> ke andar likhi hui script chalegi. 
Yeh database se saare templates nikal kar ek dropdown list banayegi.

User Interaction: User ko screen par ek dropdown dikhega jiska default option hoga "-- Create new email template --". 
User ya toh naya chunega ya kisi purane ko select karke Next dabayega.

AfterScript Execution: Next dabate hi <AfterScript> chalega, jo check karega ki agar purana template hai, 
toh uska naam memory mein save kar lo.

Transition: Uske baad workflow automatic agle step (Edit Template) par chala jayega.
*//////
()<Approval name="Select Email Template" owner="ref:requester" return="templateId,newTemplate" send="">:-
Matlab: SailPoint mein forms dikhane ke liye <Approval> tag ka use hota hai. 
Iska owner woh user hai jisne request shuru ki (requester). 
Form submit hone ke baad yeh do variables (templateId aur newTemplate) ki value ko workflow memory mein return (wapas) bhej dega.

()<Attributes>
          <Map>
            <entry key="pageTitle" value="Select Email Template"/>
            <entry key="windowWith" value="2000"/>
          </Map>
        </Attributes>
        <Button action="next" label="Next"/>
        <Button action="cancel" label="Cancel"/>:-
-->Matlab: Yeh screen ke upar ka title (heading) set kar raha hai aur window ki width (chaudai) 2000 pixel tay kar raha hai.
Matlab: Form ke neeche do buttons dikhenge—ek aage badhne ke liye (Next) aur ek cancel karne ke liye (Cancel).

()<Field displayName="Template" name="templateId" type="string" value="new">:-
Matlab: Form par ek field (dropdown box) banaya jiska naam templateId hai aur screen par uska naam Template dikhega. 
value="new" ka matlab hai ki shuruat mein isme "new" default select rahega.

()1. <Arg name="workItemType" value="Generic"/>
Yeh kya hai? Yeh SailPoint ko batata hai ki jo Form user ke samne khulne wala hai, uski category (type) kya hai.
Iska kaam: SailPoint mein alag-alag tarah ke tasks hote hain (jaise Approvals, Policy Violations, Remediations). 
Jab hum value="Generic" likhte hain, toh SailPoint isko ek Sadharan Form Task (Generic Work Item) manti hai.
Simple Bhasha mein: Yeh koi Manager ka Approval decision screen nahi hai (jahan Approve/Deny karna ho), 
balki ek simple dashboard card ya form hai jahan user ko sirf kuch fields fill karne hain ya select karna hai.
<Arg name="workItemType" value="Generic"/> me kitne type de sakte hai:-
SailPoint IdentityIQ (IIQ) me <Arg name="workItemType" value="Generic"/> me aap WorkItem.
Type Enum ki predefined values de sakte hain. SailPoint me alag-alag business processes (jaise Approvals, Remediation, Delegation) ke liye different WorkItem types hote hain.
Aap value attribute me niche diye gaye standard types use kar sakte hain:-
Common WorkItem Types:-                                                    
()Generic-----Default type.Jab koi specific business category fit nahi hoti, tab custom notifications ya general tasks ke liye ise use karte hain.
()Approval----Access Requests (LCM), Lifecycle Events, ya Roles approval ke workflows me sabse jyada use hota hai.
()Remediation----Certification/Certification Sign-off ke dauran jab koi access revoke (remediate) karna ho, 
tab ye type use hota hai.
()PolicyViolation------Jab koi Separation of Duties (SOD) ya Activity Policy violate hoti hai, 
aur us par kisi manager ya owner ka action required ho.
()Delegation-----Jab ek user apna kaam (jaise certification ya approval) kisi dusre user ko delegate karta hai.
()Challenge----Certification ke time agar koi user apne manager ke revoke decision ko challenge karta hai (Mitigation/Challenge phase).
()ViolationReview-----Policy violation ke alerts ko review aur sign-off karne ke liye.
()Form-------Jab workflow me user se intermediate input lena ho (custom forms display karne ke liye).

2. <Arg name="requester" value="ref:requester"/>:-
Yeh kya hai? Yeh ek mapping argument hai jo workflow ke global variable se data uthakar is specific form step ko deta hai.
Iska kaam: ref:requester ka matlab hai "Reference to requester". Jab workflow shuru hua tha, 
tab jis user ne isko start kiya tha (jaise aap ya koi admin), uski Identity ID requester variable mein store ho gayi thi. 
Is line ke zariye hum us ID ko is step ke andar le kar aa rahe hain.
Simple Bhasha mein: Yeh form ko batata hai ki: "Bhai, is form ko fill karne wala asli insaan kaun hai, 
uska naam/ID pakad ke rakho." Kyunki isi ke basis par form ka owner="ref:requester" taiyar hota hai aur form sahi user ke dashboard par dikhata hai.

3. <AllowedValuesDefinition> Script:-
Yeh kya hai? Yeh kisi bhi dropdown list (combo box) ka Engine hota hai.
Iska kaam: Dropdown box mein kya-kya options dikhai denge, yeh pehle se fix nahi hota. 
Yeh script database mein jaati hai aur live data ko uthakar dropdown ki list (options) taiyar karti hai.

Aapke code mein yeh kaise chal raha hai?
--Sabse pehle isne manually ek option banaya: "-- Create new email template --" (jiska backend value "new" hai).
--Fir isne context.search() chalaya aur database se saare existing EmailTemplate objects ke naam aur IDs uthaye.
--Loop chalakar un saare naamon ko list mein add kiya aur UI ko return kar diya.

////////////*
(1)setOrderBy("name") ka matlab hai: "Jo bhi data database se aayega, use name attribute ke hisaab se Alphabetical Order (A to Z) mein arrange karke laao."

-->Yeh kyun zaroori hai? (Why we use it)
Maan lijiye aapke SailPoint database mein 500 email templates hain. 
Agar aap yeh line nahi likhenge, toh database se templates bina kisi order ke (randomly) uth kar chale aayenge.
Iska asar yeh hoga ki jab user dropdown box kholega, toh use list aisi dikhegi:-
--Password Reset Notification (P se)
--Account Creation Mail (A se)
--Manager Approval Reminder (M se)
Aise random list mein se apna manpasand template dhoodhna user ke liye mushkil ho jayega.

3. Is line ke baad kya hota hai?
Kyunki aapne code mein qo.setOrderBy("name"); likha hai, isliye ab database saare templates ko A to Z format mein set karke bhejega.
Ab user ko dropdown mein templates ekdum tareeqe se dikhenge:
--Account Creation Mail
--Manager Approval Reminder
--Password Reset Notification

()context.search(EmailTemplate.class, qo, "name,id");:-
1. Pura Matlab (High-Level Explanation)
Yeh line database se kehti hai: "Mujhe EmailTemplate table mein se saare templates chahiye jo qo (QueryOptions) ki 
settings/sorting ke hisaab se hon. Lekin poora ka poora heavy object mat laana, 
mujhe sirf har template ka Name aur ID hi chahiye."

()data arraylist ke form mme save ho raha hai.
String templateName = thisTemplate[0];
String templateId = thisTemplate[1];
item=new ArrayList();
item.add(templateId);   // Index 0 par baith gaya
item.add(templateName); // Index 1 par baith gaya
Toh memory mein item ka packet kuch aisa dikhta hai: [ "0a0c11b2...", "Cellphone Certification Notification" ]

()items me bana list:-
[
  ["new", "-- Create new email template --"],
  ["id_001", "Account Creation Mail"],
  ["id_002", "Manager Approval Reminder"],
  ["id_003", "Password Reset Notification"]
]
()return items;:-
Yeh line poori script ki mehnat (saare templates ki list) ko sametkar SailPoint ke user interface (UI) ko saup deti hai, 
jisse screen par dropdown live ho jata hai. Agar aap yeh line nahi likhenge, toh dropdown khali (blank) reh jayega.
